function getStoryChapters(){
  const cls=S.char?.cls||'ninja';
  let base;
  if(cls==='samurai') base=STORY_SAMURAI;
  else if(cls==='mangaka') base=STORY_MANGA;
  else base=STORY_NINJA;
  return [...base, ...STORY_BONUS];
}

// Story chapters — each scene has full dialogue lines with JP + romaji + FR
// (kept for compatibility — replaced by getStoryChapters())
const STORY_CHAPTERS=STORY_NINJA; // fallback, dynamique via getStoryChapters()

// ── FIN STORY DATA ──


// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ══ RANGS ══
const RANKS=[
  {min:0,    name:'Débutant',  icon:'🌱', next:200},
  {min:200,  name:'Apprenti',  icon:'📜', next:600},
  {min:600,  name:'Étudiant',  icon:'🎓', next:1200},
  {min:1200, name:'Guerrier',  icon:'⚔️', next:2500},
  {min:2500, name:'Samouraï',  icon:'🥷', next:5000},
  {min:5000, name:'Maître',    icon:'🏯', next:10000},
  {min:10000,name:'Légende',   icon:'🐉', next:Infinity},
];
function getRank(xp){for(let i=RANKS.length-1;i>=0;i--)if(xp>=RANKS[i].min)return RANKS[i];return RANKS[0];}
function getRankPct(xp){const r=getRank(xp);if(r.next===Infinity)return 100;return Math.min(100,Math.round(((xp-r.min)/(r.next-r.min))*100));}

// ══ TROPHÉES ══

  {id:'srs10',      icon:'🗓️',name:'Maître SRS',     xp:80,  check:s=>Object.values(s.srs).filter(w=>w.level>=4).length>=10},
];
function checkTrophies(){
  TROPHIES.forEach(t=>{
    if(!S.trophies[t.id]&&t.check(S)){
      S.trophies[t.id]=true; addXP(t.xp);
      showToast('🏆 '+t.name+' débloqué ! +'+t.xp+'XP');
    }
  });
}

// ══ QUÊTES JOURNALIÈRES ══
const QUEST_POOL=[
  {id:'q_play3',   icon:'🎮',name:'3 parties',        desc:'Lance 3 mini-jeux',          xp:30,target:3, stat:'gamesPlayed'},
  {id:'q_words5',  icon:'📖',name:'5 nouveaux mots',  desc:'Apprends 5 mots',            xp:25,target:5, stat:'wordsLearned'},
  {id:'q_streak5', icon:'🔥',name:'Combo ×5',         desc:'5 bonnes réponses d\'affilée',xp:40,target:5, stat:'maxStreak'},
  {id:'q_kanji3',  icon:'漢',name:'3 kanji',           desc:'Quiz Kanji',                 xp:35,target:3, stat:'kanjiCount'},
  {id:'q_srs1',    icon:'🗓️',name:'Révision SRS',    desc:'Révise au moins 1 mot',       xp:20,target:1, stat:'srsToday'},
  {id:'q_story1',  icon:'📖',name:'Mode Histoire',     desc:'Joue une scène',             xp:30,target:1, stat:'storyToday'},
];
function getTodayKey(){return new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10);}
function initQuests(){
  const today=getTodayKey();
  if(S.quests&&S.quests.day===today)return;
  const picks=[...QUEST_POOL].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5).slice(0,3);
  S.quests={day:today,list:picks.map(q=>({...q,progress:0,done:false})),srsToday:0,storyToday:0};
}
function bumpQuest(stat,n=1){
  if(!S.quests)return;
  S.quests.list.forEach(q=>{
    if(!q.done&&q.stat===stat){
      if(stat==='maxStreak')q.progress=Math.max(q.progress||0,S.maxStreak);
      else q.progress=Math.min(q.target,(q.progress||0)+n);
      if(q.progress>=q.target){q.done=true;addXP(q.xp);showToast('✅ Quête : '+q.name+' +'+q.xp+'XP');}
    }
  });
}

// ══ TOAST ══
function showToast(msg){
  const d=document.createElement('div');
  d.style.cssText='position:fixed;top:68px;left:50%;transform:translateX(-50%);background:#1a0f00;color:white;border-radius:20px;padding:9px 18px;font-size:0.7rem;font-weight:700;z-index:9999;box-shadow:0 8px 24px rgba(0,0,0,0.22);animation:ptUp 2.8s ease forwards;white-space:nowrap;max-width:90vw;';
  d.textContent=msg;document.body.appendChild(d);setTimeout(()=>d.remove(),2800);
}

// SRS SYSTEM
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// 5 levels: 0=new, 1=beginner(1day), 2=inter(3days), 3=advanced(7days), 4=mastered(30days)
const SRS_INTERVALS=[0,1,3,7,30]; // days
const SRS_NAMES=['Nouveau','Débutant','Intermédiaire','Avancé','Maîtrisé'];

function srsAddWord(word){
  if(!word||!word.ro) return;
  if(S.srs[word.ro]) return; // already tracked
  S.srs[word.ro]={...word,level:0,nextReview:Date.now(),reviews:0};
}

function srsGetDue(){
  const now=Date.now();
  return Object.values(S.srs).filter(w=>w.level<4&&w.nextReview<=now);
}

function srsAnswer(ro,correct){
  if(!S.srs[ro]) return;
  const w=S.srs[ro];
  if(correct){
    w.level=Math.min(4,w.level+1);
    const days=SRS_INTERVALS[w.level];
    w.nextReview=Date.now()+(days*24*60*60*1000);
  } else {
    w.level=Math.max(0,w.level-1);
    w.nextReview=Date.now()+(60*60*1000); // retry in 1h
  }
  w.reviews++;
}

function srsCountDue(){
  return srsGetDue().length;
}

function buildSRSView(){
  const due=srsGetDue();
  const count=due.length;
  document.getElementById('srsCount').textContent=count;

  // Level breakdown
  const levels=[0,0,0,0,0];
  Object.values(S.srs).forEach(w=>levels[w.level]++);
  document.getElementById('srsLvlPill').innerHTML=SRS_NAMES.map((n,i)=>
    `<div class="srs-lvl">${n}: <span>${levels[i]}</span></div>`
  ).join('');

  if(count===0){
    document.getElementById('srsDueList').innerHTML=`
      <div class="empty-state">
        <span class="empty-icon">🌸</span>
        <div class="empty-t">Tout est à jour !</div>
        <div class="empty-s">Aucun mot à réviser pour l'instant.<br>Joue aux mini-jeux pour en ajouter.</div>
      </div>`;
    return;
  }
  document.getElementById('srsDueList').innerHTML=`
    <div class="sec-t" style="margin-bottom:12px">📋 À réviser maintenant</div>
    <div class="srs-queue">
      ${due.slice(0,12).map(w=>`
        <div class="srs-item">
          <span class="srs-due ${w.level===0?'now':w.level<3?'soon':'later'}">${SRS_NAMES[w.level]}</span>
          <span class="srs-item-jp">${w.jp}</span>
          <span class="srs-item-ro">${w.ro}</span>
          <span class="srs-item-fr">${w.fr}</span>
        </div>`).join('')}
    </div>`;
}

function updateSRSBadge(){
  const n=srsCountDue();
  const badge=document.getElementById('srsBadge');
  badge.textContent=n;badge.style.display=n>0?'inline':'none';

  const alert=document.getElementById('srsAlertHome');
  if(!alert) return;
  if(n>0){
    alert.innerHTML=`<div class="srs-alert" onclick="showView('srs')">
      <div class="srs-alert-icon">🗓️</div>
      <div><div class="srs-alert-title">${n} mot${n>1?'s':''} à réviser !</div>
        <div class="srs-alert-sub">Ta révision espacée t'attend — c'est le bon moment !</div></div>
      <div class="srs-count">${n}</div>
    </div>`;
  } else {
    alert.innerHTML='';
  }
}

let wStep=1;
function goWelcomeStep(n){
  wStep=n;
  document.querySelectorAll('.w-panel').forEach(p=>p.classList.remove('active'));
  document.getElementById(`wp${n}`).classList.add('active');
  [1,2,3].forEach(i=>{
    const d=document.getElementById(`sd${i}`);
    d.className='step-dot'+(i<n?' done':i===n?' active':'');
    d.textContent=i<n?'✓':i;
  });
  document.getElementById('welcomeBack').className='welcome-back'+(n>1?' show':'');
  document.getElementById('welcomeBack').onclick=()=>goWelcomeStep(n-1);
  if(n===3) buildConfirmCard();
}
function pickClass(el,icon,name,cls){
  document.querySelectorAll('.cls-card').forEach(c=>c.classList.remove('sel'));
  el.classList.add('sel');
  S.char={icon,name,cls};
  document.getElementById('btnStep1').disabled=false;
}
function pickGoal(el,label,icon){
  document.querySelectorAll('.goal-card').forEach(c=>c.classList.remove('sel'));
  el.classList.add('sel');
  S.goal={label,icon};
  document.getElementById('btnStep2').disabled=false;
}
function buildConfirmCard(){
  document.getElementById('confirmCard').innerHTML=`
    <div style="font-size:3rem;margin-bottom:12px">${S.char.icon}</div>
    <div style="font-family:'Kaisei Decol',serif;font-size:1.2rem;color:var(--red);margin-bottom:5px">${S.char.name}</div>
    <div style="font-size:0.65rem;color:var(--muted);margin-bottom:14px;letter-spacing:2px">${S.char.cls.toUpperCase()}</div>
    <div style="background:rgba(42,122,111,0.07);border:1.5px solid rgba(42,122,111,0.2);border-radius:10px;padding:12px;font-size:0.72rem;color:var(--teal)">
      ${S.goal.icon} Objectif : ${S.goal.label}
    </div>`;
}
function startApp(){
  document.getElementById('welcomeScreen').classList.remove('active');
  document.getElementById('appScreen').classList.add('active');
  Object.keys(COURSES).forEach(k=>S.progress[k]=new Set());
  initQuests();
  buildSidebar();buildHomeGames();buildCoursesHome();
  buildHiraView();buildKataRefView();buildKanjiView();
  buildStoryMap();updateUI();
}

const TITLES=['Débutant','Initié','Adepte','Maître','Légende'];
function updateUI(){
  const c=S.char;
  document.getElementById('navAv').textContent=c.icon;
  document.getElementById('navName').textContent=c.name;
  document.getElementById('navCls').textContent=`NV.${S.level}`;
  document.getElementById('navLv').textContent=S.level;
  document.getElementById('navStreak').textContent=S.streak;
  // XP bar shows rank progress
  document.getElementById('xpFill').style.width=getRankPct(S.xp)+'%';
  document.getElementById('heroAv').textContent=c.icon;
  document.getElementById('heroName').textContent=c.name;
  const r=getRank(S.xp);
  document.getElementById('heroBadge').textContent=`${r.icon} ${r.name} · Niveau ${S.level}`;
  document.getElementById('heroGoal').textContent=`${S.goal.icon} Objectif : ${S.goal.label}`;
  document.getElementById('sXP').textContent=S.xp;
  document.getElementById('sWords').textContent=S.wordsLearned;
  document.getElementById('sStreak').textContent=S.maxStreak;
  document.getElementById('sGames').textContent=S.gamesPlayed;
  const mc=Object.keys(S.mistakes).length;
  const mb=document.getElementById('mbBadge');
  mb.textContent=mc;mb.style.display=mc>0?'inline':'none';
  document.getElementById('mbCount').textContent=mc;
  // Rank banner on home
  const rbw=document.getElementById('rankBannerWrap');
  if(rbw){
    const pct=getRankPct(S.xp);
    rbw.innerHTML=`<div onclick="showView('stats')" style="background:linear-gradient(135deg,var(--red),#b83020);border-radius:14px;padding:12px 16px;margin-bottom:12px;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;cursor:pointer;box-shadow:0 4px 14px rgba(192,57,43,0.22)">
      <span style="font-size:1.7rem">${r.icon}</span>
      <div><div style="font-weight:900;font-size:0.85rem;color:white">${r.name}</div><div style="font-size:0.58rem;color:rgba(255,255,255,0.72)">${S.xp} XP${r.next!==Infinity?' · encore '+(r.next-S.xp)+' XP':' · MAX'}</div></div>
      <div style="margin-left:auto;text-align:right">
        <div style="width:70px;height:3px;background:rgba(255,255,255,0.2);border-radius:2px;overflow:hidden;margin-left:auto"><div style="width:${pct}%;height:100%;background:white;border-radius:2px;transition:width 0.5s"></div></div>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }
  // Quests on home
  const qw=document.getElementById('questsHomeWrap');
  if(qw&&S.quests){
    bumpQuest('maxStreak',0); // refresh streak-based quest
    qw.innerHTML=`<div class="sec-t" style="margin-bottom:8px">📅 Quêtes du jour</div>`+
      S.quests.list.map(q=>{
        const pct=Math.min(100,Math.round(((q.progress||0)/q.target)*100));
        return`<div style="background:white;border:1.5px solid rgba(0,0,0,0.09);border-radius:12px;padding:11px 13px;margin-bottom:7px;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;${q.done?'opacity:0.65;background:rgba(30,122,74,0.05)':''}">
          <span style="font-size:1.2rem">${q.icon}</span>
          <div style="flex:1;min-width:0">
            <div style="font-weight:800;font-size:0.76rem">${q.name}</div>
            <div style="font-size:0.57rem;color:var(--muted)">${q.desc}</div>
            ${!q.done?`<div style="height:3px;background:rgba(200,134,10,0.12);border-radius:2px;margin-top:4px;overflow:hidden"><div style="width:${pct}%;height:100%;background:var(--gold);border-radius:2px;transition:width 0.3s"></div></div>`
            :`<div style="font-size:0.56rem;color:var(--correct);font-weight:700;margin-top:2px">✅ Terminée !</div>`}
          </div>
          <div style="font-size:0.62rem;color:var(--gold);font-weight:800;white-space:nowrap">+${q.xp} XP</div>
        </div>`;
      }).join('');
  }
  updateSRSBadge();
  updateCoursesHome();
  checkTrophies();
}
function addXP(n){
  S.xp+=n;
  const lv=Math.floor(S.xp/120)+1;
  if(lv>S.level){S.level=lv;showLvUp();}
  updateUI();
}
function showLvUp(){
  spawnPt('🌸',8);
  const t=document.createElement('div');t.className='lvt';
  t.innerHTML=`<div class="lvt-t">🎉 NIVEAU ${S.level} !</div><div class="lvt-s">${TITLES[Math.min(S.level-1,4)]}</div>`;
  document.body.appendChild(t);setTimeout(()=>t.remove(),2600);
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// MISTAKES
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function addMistake(word){
  if(!word||!word.ro) return;
  if(S.mistakes[word.ro]) S.mistakes[word.ro].count++;
  else S.mistakes[word.ro]={...word,count:1};
  // Also add to SRS
  srsAddWord(word);
  updateUI();
}
function removeMistake(ro){delete S.mistakes[ro];updateUI();}
function buildMistakesView(){
  const keys=Object.keys(S.mistakes);
  if(keys.length===0){
    document.getElementById('mistakesContent').innerHTML=`
      <div class="empty-state"><span class="empty-icon">🌸</span>
        <div class="empty-t">Aucune erreur !</div>
        <div class="empty-s">Tu n'as pas encore fait d'erreurs.<br>Joue aux mini-jeux pour en avoir !</div>
      </div>`;return;
  }
  document.getElementById('mistakesContent').innerHTML=`
    <div class="mistake-grid">
      ${keys.map(k=>{const m=S.mistakes[k];return `<div class="mk">
        <span class="mk-jp">${m.jp}</span><span class="mk-ro">${m.ro}</span>
        <span class="mk-fr">${m.fr}</span><span class="mk-count">${m.count}×</span>
      </div>`;}).join('')}
    </div>
    <div style="display:flex;gap:10px;flex-wrap:wrap">
      <button class="btn-r" onclick="launchGame('mistakes_quiz','all')">❌ Quiz sur mes erreurs</button>
      <button class="btn-s" onclick="launchGame('srs_review','all')">🗓️ Révision SRS</button>
      <button class="btn-s" onclick="S.mistakes={};updateUI();buildMistakesView()">Tout effacer</button>
    </div>`;
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// KANA
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function buildKanaGrid(data,learnedSet,type){
  return`<div class="kana-grid">
    ${data.map(k=>`<div class="kana-cell ${learnedSet.has(k.ro)?'learned':''}" onclick="toggleKana('${type}','${k.ro}')">
      <span class="kc-jp">${k.jp}</span><span class="kc-ro">${k.ro}</span>
    </div>`).join('')}
  </div><div style="font-size:0.62rem;color:var(--muted)">${learnedSet.size}/${data.length} appris</div>`;
}
function buildHiraView(){document.getElementById('hiraContent').innerHTML=buildKanaGrid(HIRAGANA,S.hiraLearned,'hira');}
function buildKataRefView(){document.getElementById('kataRefContent').innerHTML=buildKanaGrid(KATAKANA,S.kataLearned,'kata');}
function toggleKana(type,ro){
  const set=type==='hira'?S.hiraLearned:S.kataLearned;
  if(set.has(ro))set.delete(ro);else{set.add(ro);S.wordsLearned++;}
  if(type==='hira')buildHiraView();else buildKataRefView();
  updateUI();
}

// SIDEBAR & COURSES

function buildSidebar(){
  document.getElementById('coursesSB').innerHTML=
    Object.values(COURSES).map(c=>`
      <div class="csi" id="csi-${c.id}" onclick="openCourse('${c.id}')">
        <span style="width:7px;height:7px;border-radius:50%;background:${c.color};flex-shrink:0;display:inline-block"></span>
        ${c.icon} ${c.name}
      </div>`).join('');
}
function buildHomeGames(){
  const html=GAME_DEFS.map(g=>{
    // Personnalise le Mode Histoire selon la classe
    let icon=g.icon, name=g.name, desc=g.desc;
    if(g.id==='story'){
      const cls=S.char?.cls||'ninja';
      if(cls==='ninja'){icon='🥷';name='HISTOIRE SHINOBI';desc='7 chapitres sur les ninjas et l\'ère Edo !';}
      else if(cls==='samurai'){icon='⚔️';name='HISTOIRE SAMOURAÏ';desc='7 chapitres sur le Bushido et l\'ère Edo !';}
      else if(cls==='mangaka'){icon='✏️';name='HISTOIRE MANGAKA';desc='Dragon Ball, Naruto, One Piece... rencontre les créateurs !';}
    }
    if(g.isStory){
      const done=Object.keys(S.storyProgress||{}).length;
      const total=getStoryChapters().length;
      const pct=Math.round((done/total)*100);
      const clsColor=S.char?.cls==='samurai'?'rgba(200,134,10,0.25)':S.char?.cls==='mangaka'?'rgba(74,144,217,0.25)':'rgba(124,92,191,0.25)';
      const bgGrad=S.char?.cls==='samurai'?'linear-gradient(135deg,#fffbe8,#fff0cc)':S.char?.cls==='mangaka'?'linear-gradient(135deg,#e8f4ff,#d0e8ff)':'linear-gradient(135deg,#f0e8ff,#e0d0ff)';
      return`<div class="gc" onclick="showView('story')" style="border-color:${clsColor};background:${bgGrad};grid-column:span 2">
        <span class="gc-new">HISTOIRE</span>
        <span class="gc-ico">${icon}</span>
        <div class="gc-n">${name}</div>
        <div class="gc-d">${desc}</div>
        <div style="margin-top:8px;height:4px;background:rgba(0,0,0,0.07);border-radius:2px;overflow:hidden">
          <div style="width:${pct}%;height:100%;background:var(--red);border-radius:2px;transition:width 0.5s"></div>
        </div>
        <div style="font-size:0.56rem;color:var(--muted);margin-top:3px">${done}/${total} chapitres · ${pct}%</div>
      </div>`;
    }
    if(g.isPhrases){
      if(!S.phrasesLearned)S.phrasesLearned=new Set();
      const total=100,learned=S.phrasesLearned.size,pct=Math.round((learned/total)*100);
      return`<div class="gc" onclick="showView('phrases');buildPhrasesView();" style="border-color:rgba(230,57,70,0.2);background:linear-gradient(135deg,#fff5f5,#ffe8e8);grid-column:span 2">
        <span class="gc-new">NOUVEAU</span>
        <span class="gc-ico">💬</span>
        <div class="gc-n" style="color:var(--red)">100 PHRASES DE BASE</div>
        <div class="gc-d">Tes premieres phrases au Japon — 10 categories !</div>
        <div style="margin-top:8px;height:4px;background:rgba(0,0,0,0.07);border-radius:2px;overflow:hidden">
          <div style="width:${pct}%;height:100%;background:var(--red);border-radius:2px;transition:width 0.5s"></div>
        </div>
        <div style="font-size:0.56rem;color:var(--muted);margin-top:3px">${learned}/${total} phrases apprises · ${pct}%</div>
      </div>`;
    }
    const onclick=g.isMistake?`launchGame('mistakes_quiz','all')`:
                  g.isStory?`showView('story')`:
                  g.isPhrases?`showView('phrases');buildPhrasesView()`:
                  `launchGame('${g.id}','${g.theme||'all'}')`;
    return`<div class="gc" onclick="${onclick}">
      ${g.isNew?'<span class="gc-new">NOUVEAU</span>':''}
      <span class="gc-ico">${icon}</span>
      <div class="gc-n">${name}</div>
      <div class="gc-d">${desc}</div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
  document.getElementById('homeGamesGrid').innerHTML=html;
  document.getElementById('allGamesGrid').innerHTML=html;
}
function updateCoursesHome(){
  const allK=typeof KANJI_LEVELS_ALL!=="undefined"?KANJI_LEVELS_ALL.flatMap(l=>l.kanji):KANJI_LIST;
const kl=S.kanjiLearned.size,kt=allK.length,kp=Math.round((kl/kt)*100);
  document.getElementById('coursesHomeGrid').innerHTML=
    `<div class="cc" onclick="showView('kanji')" style="border-color:rgba(123,79,158,0.22)">
      <div class="cc-ico">漢</div>
      <div class="cc-info"><div class="cc-n">Kanji JLPT N5</div>
        <div class="cc-cnt">${kt} kanji · ${kl} appris</div>
        <div class="cc-bw"><div class="cc-bf" style="width:${kp}%;background:#7b4f9e"></div></div>
        <div class="cc-pct">${kp}%</div></div>
    </div>`+
    Object.values(COURSES).map(c=>{
      const l=S.progress[c.id]?.size||0,t=c.words.length,pct=Math.round((l/t)*100);
      return`<div class="cc" onclick="openCourse('${c.id}')" style="border-color:rgba(${hexRgb(c.color)},0.18)">
        <div class="cc-ico">${c.icon}</div>
        <div class="cc-info"><div class="cc-n">${c.name}</div>
          <div class="cc-cnt">${t} mots · ${l} appris</div>
          <div class="cc-bw"><div class="cc-bf" style="width:${pct}%;background:${c.color}"></div></div>
          <div class="cc-pct">${pct}%</div></div>
      </div>`;}).join('');
}
function buildCoursesHome(){updateCoursesHome();}

function hexRgb(h){
  const r=parseInt(h.slice(1,3),16),g=parseInt(h.slice(3,5),16),b=parseInt(h.slice(5,7),16);
  return`${r},${g},${b}`;
}
function openCourse(id){
  const c=COURSES[id];showView('course');
  document.querySelectorAll('.csi').forEach(e=>e.classList.remove('active'));
  document.getElementById(`csi-${id}`)?.classList.add('active');
  const learned=S.progress[id]||new Set();
  const pct=Math.round((learned.size/c.words.length)*100);
  document.getElementById('courseContent').innerHTML=`
    <div style="background:linear-gradient(135deg,#fff5e8,#ffe8d8);border:2px solid var(--border2);border-radius:16px;padding:20px 24px;margin-bottom:18px;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:16px">
      <div style="font-size:2.5rem">${c.icon}</div>
      <div style="flex:1">
        <div style="font-family:'Kaisei Decol',serif;font-size:1.1rem;color:var(--red);margin-bottom:2px">${c.name}</div>
        <div style="font-size:0.66rem;color:var(--muted);margin-bottom:8px">${c.words.length} mots</div>
        <div style="height:4px;background:rgba(180,120,60,0.15);border-radius:2px;overflow:hidden;max-width:240px">
          <div style="width:${pct}%;height:100%;background:${c.color};border-radius:2px;transition:width 0.5s"></div>
        </div>
        <div style="font-size:0.6rem;color:var(--muted);margin-top:3px">${learned.size}/${c.words.length} · ${pct}%</div>
      </div>
      <button class="btn-r" onclick="launchGame('qcm','${id}')">▶ S'entraîner</button>
    </div>
    <div class="sec-t">📝 Vocabulaire</div>
    <div class="words-grid">
      ${c.words.map(w=>`
        <div class="wc ${learned.has(w.ro)?'learned':''}" onclick="markLearned('${id}','${w.ro}')">
          <span class="wc-jp">${w.jp}
            <button class="w-audio" onclick="event.stopPropagation();speakJP('${w.jp}')" title="Écouter">🔊</button>
          </span>
          <span class="wc-ro">${w.ro}</span>
          <span class="wc-fr">${w.fr}</span>
        </div>`).join('')}
    </div>
    <div style="font-size:0.62rem;color:var(--muted);margin-bottom:14px">💡 Clique pour marquer comme appris</div>
    <div style="display:flex;gap:10px;flex-wrap:wrap">
      <button class="btn-r" onclick="launchGame('qcm','${id}')">🎯 QCM</button>
      <button class="btn-s" onclick="launchGame('audio_game','${id}')">🔊 Audio</button>
      <button class="btn-s" onclick="launchGame('order','${id}')">🔀 Mot mélangé</button>
    </div>`;
}
function markLearned(id,ro){
  S.progress[id].add(ro);S.wordsLearned++;
  const word=COURSES[id]?.words.find(w=>w.ro===ro);
  if(word) srsAddWord(word);
  updateUI();openCourse(id);
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// KANJI VIEW
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function buildKanjiView(){
  const ALL_LEVELS=typeof KANJI_LEVELS_ALL!=="undefined"?KANJI_LEVELS_ALL:KANJI_LEVELS;
  const totalK=ALL_LEVELS.flatMap(l=>l.kanji).length;
  const l=S.kanjiLearned.size,t=totalK;
  const pct=Math.round((l/t)*100);
  const pf=document.getElementById('kanjiPF');
  const pt=document.getElementById('kanjiPCT');
  if(pf)pf.style.width=pct+'%';
  if(pt)pt.textContent=`${l} / ${totalK}`;
  const cont=document.getElementById('kanjiLevels');
  if(!cont)return;
  cont.innerHTML=ALL_LEVELS.map((lv,li)=>{
    const lvL=lv.kanji.filter(k=>S.kanjiLearned.has(k.k)).length;
    const lvP=Math.round((lvL/lv.kanji.length)*100);
    const offset=ALL_LEVELS.slice(0,li).reduce((a,l)=>a+l.kanji.length,0);
    return`<div class="kanji-level-section">
      <div class="kanji-level-header" onclick="toggleKanjiLevel(${li})">
        <div class="klh-num ${lvP===100?'done':''}" style="${lvP!==100?'border-color:'+lv.color+';color:'+lv.color:''}">
          ${lvP===100?'✓':li+1}</div>
        <div class="klh-info">
          <div class="klh-title">${lv.deco} ${lv.title}</div>
          <div class="klh-sub">${lv.kanji.length} kanji · ${lvL} appris</div>
        </div>
        <div class="klh-prog" style="color:${lv.color}">${lvP}%</div>
        <div class="klh-arrow" id="arr${li}">▶</div>
      </div>
      <div class="kanji-level-grid ${li===0?'open':''}" id="klg${li}">
        ${lv.kanji.map((kj,i)=>`
          <div class="kj-card ${S.kanjiLearned.has(kj.k)?'learned':''}" onclick="openKanji(${offset+i})">
            <span class="kj-check">✓</span>
            <span class="kj-deco">${kj.deco}</span>
            <span class="kj-kanji">${kj.k}</span>
            <div class="kj-on">${kj.on}</div>
            <div class="kj-kun">${kj.kun}</div>
            <div class="kj-fr">${kj.fr}</div>
            <span class="kj-stroke">${kj.strokes}tr.</span>
          </div>`).join('')}
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}
function toggleKanjiLevel(i){
  document.getElementById(`klg${i}`).classList.toggle('open');
  document.getElementById(`arr${i}`).classList.toggle('open');
}
function openKanji(idx){
  const allKanjiList=typeof KANJI_LEVELS_ALL!=="undefined"?KANJI_LEVELS_ALL.flatMap(l=>l.kanji):KANJI_LIST;
const kj=allKanjiList[idx];
  const ov=document.createElement('div');ov.className='kj-modal-overlay';ov.id='kjOverlay';
  ov.onclick=e=>{if(e.target===ov)closeKanjiModal();};
  ov.innerHTML=`
    <div class="kj-modal">
      <button class="kj-modal-close" onclick="closeKanjiModal()">✕</button>
      <span class="kj-modal-kanji">${kj.k}</span>
      <div class="kj-modal-meaning">${kj.fr}</div>
      <div class="kj-modal-row">
        <span class="kj-tag">音 ${kj.on}</span>
        <span class="kj-tag teal">訓 ${kj.kun}</span>
        <span class="kj-tag gold">${kj.strokes} traits</span>
      </div>
      <div class="kj-modal-example">
        <div style="margin-bottom:6px;font-size:0.6rem;color:var(--muted);letter-spacing:1px">EXEMPLES</div>
        <strong>${kj.ex}</strong>
        <div style="margin-top:10px;border-top:1px solid var(--border2);padding-top:10px">
          <div style="font-family:'Noto Sans JP',sans-serif;font-size:1rem;margin-bottom:3px;color:var(--ink)">${kj.ex_jp}</div>
          <div style="font-size:0.68rem;color:var(--muted)">${kj.ex_fr}</div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="kj-modal-btns">
        <button class="btn-r" onclick="speakJP('${kj.k}');this.textContent='🔊…';setTimeout(()=>this.textContent='🔊 Écouter',1500)">🔊 Écouter</button>
        <button class="${S.kanjiLearned.has(kj.k)?'btn-s':'btn-r'}" id="kjLearnBtn" onclick="toggleKanjiLearned('${kj.k}',this)">
          ${S.kanjiLearned.has(kj.k)?'✓ Appris':'Marquer appris'}</button>
        <button class="btn-s" onclick="closeKanjiModal();launchGame('kanji_quiz','all')">▶ Quiz</button>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  document.body.appendChild(ov);speakJP(kj.k);
}
function closeKanjiModal(){document.getElementById('kjOverlay')?.remove();}
function toggleKanjiLearned(k,btn){
  if(S.kanjiLearned.has(k)){
    S.kanjiLearned.delete(k);btn.textContent='Marquer appris';btn.className='btn-r';
  } else {
    S.kanjiLearned.add(k);S.wordsLearned++;
    const allKanjiList2=typeof KANJI_LEVELS_ALL!=="undefined"?KANJI_LEVELS_ALL.flatMap(l=>l.kanji):KANJI_LIST;
const kj=allKanjiList2.find(x=>x.k===k);
    if(kj) srsAddWord({jp:kj.k,ro:kj.kun.split('・')[0],fr:kj.fr});
    btn.textContent='✓ Appris';btn.className='btn-s';spawnPt('漢',2);
  }
  buildKanjiView();updateUI();
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// VIEWS
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function showView(name){
  document.querySelectorAll('.view').forEach(v=>v.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.si').forEach(s=>s.classList.remove('active'));
  document.getElementById(`view-${name}`)?.classList.add('active');
  document.getElementById(`si-${name}`)?.classList.add('active');
  if(name==='mistakes')buildMistakesView();
  if(name==='srs'){buildSRSView();}
  if(name==='story')buildStoryMap();
  if(name==='stats')buildStatsView();
  window.scrollTo(0,0);
}
function buildStatsView(){
  const r=getRank(S.xp),pct=getRankPct(S.xp);
  const rc=document.getElementById('statsRankCard');
  if(rc) rc.innerHTML=`<div style="background:linear-gradient(135deg,var(--red),#b83020);border-radius:16px;padding:18px;color:white;box-shadow:0 6px 22px rgba(192,57,43,0.22)">
    <div style="font-size:2rem;margin-bottom:4px">${r.icon}</div>
    <div style="font-weight:900;font-size:1.4rem;margin-bottom:2px">${r.name}</div>
    <div style="font-size:0.62rem;opacity:0.75;margin-bottom:12px">${S.xp} XP${r.next!==Infinity?' · encore '+(r.next-S.xp)+' XP pour le rang suivant':' · Rang maximum !'}</div>
    <div style="height:6px;background:rgba(255,255,255,0.2);border-radius:3px;overflow:hidden"><div style="width:${pct}%;height:100%;background:white;border-radius:3px;transition:width 0.6s"></div></div>
  </div>`;
  const tg=document.getElementById('statsTrophyGrid');
  if(tg) tg.innerHTML=TROPHIES.map(t=>`
    <div style="background:white;border:1.5px solid ${S.trophies[t.id]?'rgba(200,134,10,0.35)':'var(--border2)'};border-radius:12px;padding:10px 5px;text-align:center;${S.trophies[t.id]?'background:rgba(200,134,10,0.06)':''}" title="${t.id}">
      <span style="font-size:1.4rem;display:block;margin-bottom:3px;${!S.trophies[t.id]?'filter:grayscale(1);opacity:0.25':''}">${t.icon}</span>
      <div style="font-size:0.5rem;font-weight:700;color:${S.trophies[t.id]?'var(--text2)':'var(--muted2)'};line-height:1.4">${t.name}</div>
      <div style="font-size:0.48rem;color:var(--gold);font-weight:700;margin-top:2px">${S.trophies[t.id]?'✓':'+'+t.xp+' XP'}</div>
    </div>`).join('');
  const cb=document.getElementById('statsCoursesBars');
  if(cb) cb.innerHTML=Object.values(COURSES).map(c=>{
    const l=S.progress[c.id]?.size||0,t=c.words.length,p=Math.round((l/t)*100);
    return`<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;font-size:0.63rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--muted);margin-bottom:3px"><span>${c.icon} ${c.name}</span><span style="color:${c.color}">${p}%</span></div>
    <div style="height:5px;background:rgba(0,0,0,0.06);border-radius:3px;overflow:hidden;margin-bottom:9px"><div style="width:${p}%;height:100%;background:${c.color};border-radius:3px;transition:width 0.7s"></div></div>`;
  }).join('');
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// STORY MODE
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function buildStoryMap(){
  // Header dynamique selon la classe
  const cls=S.char?.cls||'ninja';
  const storyMeta={
    ninja: {icon:'🥷',title:'Histoire Shinobi',sub:'Deviens un ninja légendaire de l\'ère Edo',color:'var(--violet)',bg:'linear-gradient(135deg,var(--violet),#6a3db8)'},
    samurai:{icon:'⚔️',title:'Histoire Samouraï',sub:'Maîtrise le Bushido et l\'honneur du clan',color:'var(--gold)',bg:'linear-gradient(135deg,var(--gold),#c87000)'},
    mangaka:{icon:'✏️',title:'Histoire Mangaka',sub:'Rencontre les créateurs de Dragon Ball, Naruto, One Piece',color:'var(--blue)',bg:'linear-gradient(135deg,var(--blue),#2d50a6)'},
  }[cls]||{icon:'📖',title:'Mode Histoire',sub:'Apprends le japonais à travers une aventure',color:'var(--red)',bg:'linear-gradient(135deg,var(--red),var(--orange))'};
  document.getElementById('storyViewHeader').innerHTML=`
    <div style="background:${storyMeta.bg};border-radius:20px;padding:20px 22px;margin-bottom:20px;color:white;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:14px;box-shadow:0 8px 26px rgba(0,0,0,0.15)">
      <div style="font-size:3rem">${storyMeta.icon}</div>
      <div>
        <div style="font-family:'Kaisei Decol',serif;font-size:1.2rem;font-weight:800;margin-bottom:4px">${storyMeta.title}</div>
        <div style="font-size:0.65rem;opacity:0.85">${storyMeta.sub}</div>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  getStoryChapters().forEach((ch,i)=>{
    if(i===0) ch.status='active';
    else if(S.storyProgress[i-1]) ch.status='available';
    else ch.status='locked';
  });

  document.getElementById('storyMap').innerHTML=`
    <div class="story-map">
      <div class="story-path"></div>
      ${getStoryChapters().map((ch,i)=>{
        const done=!!S.storyProgress[i];
        const locked=ch.status==='locked';
        const nodeClass=done?'done':ch.status==='active'?'active':ch.status==='available'?'available':'locked';
        return`<div class="story-chapter">
          <div class="story-node ${nodeClass}" onclick="${!locked?`playStory(${i})`:''}">
            ${done?'✓':ch.icon}
          </div>
          <div class="story-card-wrap">
            <div class="story-card ${locked?'locked-card':''}" onclick="${!locked?`playStory(${i})`:''}">
              <div class="story-card-ico">${ch.icon}</div>
              <div class="story-card-title">${ch.title}</div>
              <div class="story-card-sub">${ch.sub}</div>
              <div class="story-card-xp">+${ch.xp} XP${done?' · ✓ Complété':locked?' · 🔒 Verrouillé':''}</div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>`;
      }).join('')}
    </div>`;
}

// ── STORY ENGINE v7 — scrolling lines + audio + double-tap ──
let storyState={chIdx:0,scIdx:0,lineIdx:0,answered:false,lastTap:0,lastTapIdx:-1};

function playStory(chIdx){
  showView('game');
  storyState={chIdx,scIdx:0,lineIdx:0,answered:false,lastTap:0,lastTapIdx:-1};
  renderStoryScene();
}

function renderStoryScene(){
  const ch=getStoryChapters()[storyState.chIdx];
  const sc=ch.scenes[storyState.scIdx];
  const total=ch.scenes.length;
  const progress=Math.round((storyState.scIdx/total)*100);
  storyState.lineIdx=0;storyState.answered=false;storyState.lastTap=0;storyState.lastTapIdx=-1;

  document.getElementById('gameWrap').innerHTML=`
    <div class="gh">
      <button class="g-back" onclick="showView('story')">← Histoire</button>
      <div class="g-ta"><div class="g-ti">${ch.icon} ${ch.title}</div><div class="g-su">Scène ${storyState.scIdx+1} / ${total}</div></div>
      <div style="font-size:0.7rem;color:var(--muted)">+${ch.xp} XP</div>
    </div>
    <div class="gpb"><div class="gpf" style="width:${progress}%"></div></div>

    <div class="story-dlg">
      <div class="story-speaker">
        <div class="story-av">${sc.speaker}</div>
        <div><div class="story-sname">${sc.name}</div><div class="story-srole">${sc.role}</div></div>
      </div>
      <div class="story-lines" id="storyLines"></div>
      <div id="storyLineNav" style="text-align:center;margin-top:8px">
        <button class="audio-btn" id="nextLineBtn" onclick="showNextLine()" style="font-size:0.68rem;padding:7px 18px">
          ▶ Écouter la suite
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div id="storyChoicesWrap" style="display:none">
      <div style="font-size:0.68rem;color:var(--muted);margin-bottom:10px;letter-spacing:1px">
        💬 Comment répondre ? <span style="color:var(--muted2)">(double-clic = passer automatiquement)</span>
      </div>
      <div class="story-choices" id="storyChoices">
        ${sc.choices.map((c,i)=>`<button class="story-choice" id="sc${i}" onclick="tapStory(${i})">${c}</button>`).join('')}
      </div>
      <div class="fb" id="fb"></div>
      <button class="nb" id="nb" onclick="nextStoryScene()">${storyState.scIdx+1<total?'Scène suivante →':'Terminer le chapitre !'}</button>
    </div>`;

  // Auto-show first line
  showNextLine();
}

function showNextLine(){
  const ch=getStoryChapters()[storyState.chIdx];
  const sc=ch.scenes[storyState.scIdx];
  const lines=sc.lines;
  const idx=storyState.lineIdx;

  if(idx>=lines.length){
    document.getElementById('storyLineNav').style.display='none';
    document.getElementById('storyChoicesWrap').style.display='block';
    return;
  }

  const ln=lines[idx];
  const linesContainer=document.getElementById('storyLines');

  linesContainer.querySelectorAll('.story-line').forEach(el=>el.classList.remove('active'));

  const div=document.createElement('div');
  div.className='story-line active';
  const safeJp=ln.jp.replace(/'/g,"\\'").replace(/"/g,'&quot;');
  div.innerHTML=`
    <span class="story-line-jp">${ln.jp}
      <button class="story-line-audio" onclick="speakJP('${safeJp}')">🔊</button>
    </span>
    <span class="story-line-ro">${ln.ro}</span>
    <span class="story-line-fr">${ln.fr}</span>`;
  linesContainer.appendChild(div);
  storyState.lineIdx++;

  const speakDelay=storyState.lineIdx===1?500:150;
  setTimeout(()=>{
    speakJP(ln.jp);
    setTimeout(()=>{ linesContainer.scrollTop=linesContainer.scrollHeight; },100);
  }, speakDelay);

  const btn=document.getElementById('nextLineBtn');
  if(btn){
    btn.disabled=true;
    btn.textContent='⏳ En cours…';
    const ms=Math.max(1400, ln.jp.length*320);
    setTimeout(()=>{
      if(!document.getElementById('nextLineBtn')) return;
      btn.disabled=false;
      if(storyState.lineIdx>=lines.length){
        btn.textContent='💬 Voir les choix de réponse';
        btn.style.background='rgba(192,57,43,0.08)';
        btn.style.color='var(--red)';
        btn.style.borderColor='rgba(192,57,43,0.3)';
      } else {
        btn.textContent=`▶ Ligne suivante (${storyState.lineIdx+1}/${lines.length})`;
        btn.style.background='';btn.style.color='';btn.style.borderColor='';
      }
    }, ms);
  }
}

function tapStory(i){
  const now=Date.now();
  const sc=getStoryChapters()[storyState.chIdx].scenes[storyState.scIdx];

  if(storyState.answered) return;

  // Highlight on first tap
  document.querySelectorAll('.story-choice').forEach((b,idx)=>{
    b.style.opacity= idx===i?'1':'0.55';
  });
  document.getElementById(`sc${i}`).style.borderColor='var(--gold)';
  document.getElementById(`sc${i}`).style.background='rgba(200,134,10,0.07)';

  const isDouble = (now - storyState.lastTap < 500) && storyState.lastTapIdx===i;
  storyState.lastTap=now;
  storyState.lastTapIdx=i;

  if(isDouble){
    // Confirm answer
    answerStory(i);
  } else {
    // Show hint
    const hint=document.getElementById('fb');
    if(hint){hint.className='fb show';hint.style.background='rgba(200,134,10,0.07)';hint.style.border='1px solid rgba(200,134,10,0.2)';hint.style.color='var(--gold)';hint.innerHTML='👆 Double-clic pour confirmer !';}
  }
}

function answerStory(i){
  if(storyState.answered)return;
  storyState.answered=true;
  const sc=getStoryChapters()[storyState.chIdx].scenes[storyState.scIdx];
  document.querySelectorAll('.story-choice').forEach(b=>{b.disabled=true;b.style.opacity='1';b.style.borderColor='';b.style.background='';});
  document.getElementById(`sc${i}`).classList.add(i===sc.correct?'correct':'wrong');
  if(i!==sc.correct) document.getElementById(`sc${sc.correct}`).classList.add('correct');
  const ok=i===sc.correct;
  if(ok){S.streak++;S.maxStreak=Math.max(S.maxStreak,S.streak);addXP(10);spawnPt('🌸',3);}
  else{S.streak=0;}
  const fb=document.getElementById('fb');
  if(fb){fb.style='';fb.className=`fb show ${ok?'ok':'bad'}`;fb.innerHTML=`<div class="fb-t">${ok?'正解！ ✓':'惜しい… ✗'}</div>${sc.explain}`;}
  document.getElementById('nb').classList.add('show');
  updateUI();
}

function nextStoryScene(){
  const ch=getStoryChapters()[storyState.chIdx];
  storyState.scIdx++;storyState.lineIdx=0;storyState.answered=false;storyState.lastTap=0;storyState.lastTapIdx=-1;
  if(storyState.scIdx>=ch.scenes.length){
    S.storyProgress[storyState.chIdx]=true;
    addXP(ch.xp);spawnPt('⭐',6);
    document.getElementById('gameWrap').innerHTML=`
      <div class="es">
        <div class="es-ring">🌸</div>
        <div class="es-title">Chapitre terminé !</div>
        <span class="es-xp">+${ch.xp} XP</span>
        <div class="es-msg">${ch.title} complété ✅<br>Tu maîtrises maintenant les dialogues de cette situation au Japon !</div>
        <div style="background:rgba(42,122,111,0.07);border:1.5px solid rgba(42,122,111,0.2);border-radius:12px;padding:12px;font-size:0.68rem;color:var(--teal);margin-bottom:16px;cursor:pointer" onclick="showSaveModal()">
          💾 Pense à sauvegarder ta progression !
        </div>
        <div class="es-btns">
          <button class="btn-r" onclick="showView('story')">📖 Carte de l'histoire</button>
          <button class="btn-s" onclick="showView('home')">Accueil</button>
        </div>
      </div>`;
    buildStoryMap();
  } else renderStoryScene();
}


// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// AUDIO
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function speakJP(text){
  if(!window.speechSynthesis) return;
  window.speechSynthesis.cancel();
  const trySpeak=()=>{
    const u=new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);
    u.lang='ja-JP'; u.rate=0.82; u.pitch=1.0;
    const voices=window.speechSynthesis.getVoices();
    const jv=voices.find(v=>v.lang==='ja-JP')||voices.find(v=>v.lang.startsWith('ja'));
    if(jv) u.voice=jv;
    window.speechSynthesis.speak(u);
  };
  // If voices not yet loaded, wait
  if(window.speechSynthesis.getVoices().length===0){
    window.speechSynthesis.onvoiceschanged=()=>{ trySpeak(); };
    setTimeout(trySpeak, 600); // fallback
  } else {
    trySpeak();
  }
}
function audioBtn(text){
  return`<button class="audio-btn" onclick="speakJP('${text}');this.classList.add('playing');setTimeout(()=>this.classList.remove('playing'),1400)">
    <span class="wave-bars"><span class="wb"></span><span class="wb"></span><span class="wb"></span><span class="wb"></span></span> Écouter
  </button>`;
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// GAME LAUNCHER
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function launchGame(type,theme='all'){
  S.gamesPlayed++;
  bumpQuest('gamesPlayed');
  showView('game');
  if(type==='qcm')startQCM(theme);
  else if(type==='blank')startBlank();
  else if(type==='kata_game')startKataGame(theme);
  else if(type==='memo')startMemo();
  else if(type==='order')startOrder(theme);
  else if(type==='flash')startFlash();
  else if(type==='kanji_quiz')startKanjiQuiz();
  else if(type==='audio_game')startAudioGame(theme);
  else if(type==='srs_review')startSRSReview();
  else if(type==='mistakes_quiz')startMistakesQuiz();
  else if(type==='cuisine')startCuisine();
  else if(type==='rain')startRain();
  else if(type==='intrus')startIntrus();
  else if(type==='chrono')startChrono();
  else if(type==='traduction')startTraduction(theme);
  else if(type==='phrases'){showView('phrases');buildPhrasesView();}
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// QCM
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function buildQCM(theme){
  // Toujours piocher dans TOUS les cours pour plus de variété
  const pool=Object.values(COURSES).flatMap(c=>c.words);
  return[...pool].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5).slice(0,8).map(w=>{
    const wrongs=pool.filter(x=>x.fr!==w.fr).sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5).slice(0,3);
    const opts=[...wrongs,w].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5);
    return{word:w,opts,correct:opts.findIndex(o=>o.fr===w.fr),xp:12,expl:`${w.jp} (${w.ro}) = ${w.fr}`};
  });
}
function startQCM(theme){const qs=buildQCM(theme);S.gs={type:'qcm',qs,idx:0,score:0,lives:3,answered:false,theme};renderQCM();}
function renderQCM(){
  const gs=S.gs;const q=gs.qs[gs.idx];
  document.getElementById('gameWrap').innerHTML=`
    ${gHeader('🎯 Chasse au Mot',gs.idx+1,gs.qs.length,gs.lives)}
    <div class="gpb"><div class="gpf" style="width:${(gs.idx/gs.qs.length)*100}%"></div></div>
    <div class="qc"><div class="qt red">● VOCABULAIRE</div>
      <div class="q-ctr">
        <div class="q-ctx">Que signifie ce mot ?</div>
        <div class="q-w">${q.word.jp}</div>
        <div class="q-ro">${q.word.ro}</div>
        ${audioBtn(q.word.jp)}
      </div>
      <div class="og">${q.opts.map((o,i)=>`<button class="opt" id="o${i}" onclick="ansQCM(${i})">
        <span class="oj">${o.jp}</span><span class="of">${o.fr}</span>
      </button>`).join('')}</div>
    </div>
    <div class="fb" id="fb"></div>
    <button class="nb" id="nb" onclick="nextQCM()">SUIVANT →</button>`;
}
// Double-tap tracker for games
let _lastTap={t:0,i:-1};
function doubleTap(i,cb){
  const now=Date.now();
  // Highlight selected
  document.querySelectorAll('.opt').forEach((b,idx)=>{
    b.style.opacity=idx===i?'1':'0.55';
    b.style.borderColor='';
  });
  const btn=document.getElementById(`o${i}`);
  if(btn){btn.style.borderColor='var(--gold)';btn.style.background='rgba(200,134,10,0.07)';}
  if((now-_lastTap.t)<500 && _lastTap.i===i){
    _lastTap={t:0,i:-1};
    document.querySelectorAll('.opt').forEach(b=>{b.style.opacity='1';b.style.borderColor='';b.style.background='';});
    cb();
  } else {
    _lastTap={t:now,i};
    const fb=document.getElementById('fb');
    if(fb){fb.className='fb show';fb.style.cssText='background:rgba(200,134,10,0.07);border:1px solid rgba(200,134,10,0.2);color:var(--gold)';fb.innerHTML='👆 Double-clic pour confirmer !';}
  }
}

function ansQCM(i){
  const gs=S.gs;if(gs.answered)return;
  doubleTap(i,()=>{
    gs.answered=true;
    const q=gs.qs[gs.idx];
    document.querySelectorAll('.opt').forEach(b=>b.disabled=true);
    if(i===q.correct){
      document.getElementById(`o${i}`).classList.add('ok');
      gs.score+=q.xp;S.streak++;S.maxStreak=Math.max(S.maxStreak,S.streak);S.wordsLearned++;
      if(gs.theme!=='all')S.progress[gs.theme]?.add(q.word.ro);
      srsAddWord(q.word);srsAnswer(q.word.ro,true);
      addXP(q.xp);spawnPt('🌸',3);showFb(true,q.expl);
    } else {
      document.getElementById(`o${i}`).classList.add('bad');
      document.getElementById(`o${q.correct}`).classList.add('ok');
      gs.lives--;S.streak=0;addMistake(q.word);srsAnswer(q.word.ro,false);
      showFb(false,q.expl,`Bonne réponse : ${q.opts[q.correct].fr}`);
    }
    updateUI();document.getElementById('nb').classList.add('show');
    // Auto-advance after 1.4s
    setTimeout(()=>{if(document.getElementById('nb'))nextQCM();},1400);
  });
}
function nextQCM(){
  const gs=S.gs;gs.idx++;gs.answered=false;
  if(gs.idx>=gs.qs.length||gs.lives<=0)endGame(gs.score,gs.qs.length,'qcm',gs.theme);
  else renderQCM();
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// BLANK
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function startBlank(){S.gs={type:'blank',qs:[...BLANK_QS].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5),idx:0,score:0,lives:3,answered:false};renderBlank();}
function renderBlank(){
  const gs=S.gs;const q=gs.qs[gs.idx];
  document.getElementById('gameWrap').innerHTML=`
    ${gHeader('✍️ Phrase Brisée',gs.idx+1,gs.qs.length,gs.lives)}
    <div class="gpb"><div class="gpf" style="width:${(gs.idx/gs.qs.length)*100}%"></div></div>
    <div class="qc"><div class="qt teal">● COMPLÈTE</div>
      <div class="q-ctr">
        <div class="q-sen">${q.display}</div>
        <div class="q-tr">🇫🇷 ${q.trans}</div>
      </div>
      <div style="font-size:0.62rem;color:var(--muted);margin-bottom:7px">💡 ${q.hint}</div>
      <div class="tr">
        <input class="ti" id="bi" placeholder="Ta réponse..." onkeydown="if(event.key==='Enter')ansBlank()">
        <button class="tok" onclick="ansBlank()">OK</button>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="fb" id="fb"></div>
    <button class="nb" id="nb" onclick="nextBlank()">SUIVANT →</button>`;
  setTimeout(()=>document.getElementById('bi')?.focus(),80);
}
function ansBlank(){
  const gs=S.gs;if(gs.answered)return;
  const q=gs.qs[gs.idx];
  const val=document.getElementById('bi').value.trim().toLowerCase();
  const ok=val===q.answer.toLowerCase()||val===q.ro.toLowerCase();
  gs.answered=true;document.getElementById('bi').disabled=true;
  if(ok){document.getElementById('bi').style.borderColor='var(--correct)';gs.score+=q.xp;S.wordsLearned++;addXP(q.xp);spawnPt('🌸',3);showFb(true,q.expl);}
  else{document.getElementById('bi').style.borderColor='var(--wrong)';gs.lives--;S.streak=0;addMistake({jp:q.answer,ro:q.ro,fr:q.answer});showFb(false,q.expl,`Réponse : ${q.answer} (${q.ro})`);}
  updateUI();document.getElementById('nb').classList.add('show');
}
function nextBlank(){
  const gs=S.gs;gs.idx++;gs.answered=false;
  if(gs.idx>=gs.qs.length||gs.lives<=0)endGame(gs.score,gs.qs.length,'blank','all');
  else renderBlank();
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// KANA GAME
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function startKataGame(type){
  const pool=type==='hira'?HIRAGANA:KATAKANA;
  const qs=[...pool].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5).slice(0,14);
  S.gs={type:'kata_game',qs,idx:0,score:0,lives:3,answered:false,timerInt:null,ktype:type};
  renderKataGame();
}
function renderKataGame(){
  const gs=S.gs;const q=gs.qs[gs.idx];
  clearInterval(gs.timerInt);
  const label=gs.ktype==='hira'?'あ HIRAGANA':'ア KATAKANA';
  document.getElementById('gameWrap').innerHTML=`
    ${gHeader(`${label} → Romaji`,gs.idx+1,gs.qs.length,gs.lives)}
    <div class="gpb"><div class="gpf" style="width:${(gs.idx/gs.qs.length)*100}%"></div></div>
    <div class="qc"><div class="qt violet">● KANA → ROMAJI</div>
      <div class="kata-box"><span class="kata-ch" id="kch">${q.jp}</span><div class="kata-hint">Écris en romaji</div></div>
      <div class="ktb"><div class="ktf" id="ktf" style="width:100%"></div></div>
      <div class="tr">
        <input class="ti" id="ki" placeholder="romaji..." maxlength="5" onkeydown="if(event.key==='Enter')ansKana()">
        <button class="tok" onclick="ansKana()">OK</button>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="fb" id="fb"></div>
    <button class="nb" id="nb" onclick="nextKana()">SUIVANT →</button>`;
  let t=100;
  gs.timerInt=setInterval(()=>{
    t-=1.8;const el=document.getElementById('ktf');
    if(el)el.style.width=t+'%';
    if(t<=0){clearInterval(gs.timerInt);if(!gs.answered){
      gs.answered=true;gs.lives--;
      const inp=document.getElementById('ki');if(inp)inp.disabled=true;
      addMistake({jp:q.jp,ro:q.ro,fr:q.ro});
      showFb(false,'Temps écoulé !',`La réponse était : ${q.ro}`);
      document.getElementById('nb')?.classList.add('show');updateUI();
    }}
  },100);
  setTimeout(()=>document.getElementById('ki')?.focus(),80);
}
function ansKana(){
  const gs=S.gs;if(gs.answered)return;
  clearInterval(gs.timerInt);
  const q=gs.qs[gs.idx];const val=document.getElementById('ki').value.trim().toLowerCase();
  const ok=val===q.ro;gs.answered=true;document.getElementById('ki').disabled=true;
  const tf=document.getElementById('ktf');if(tf)tf.style.transition='none';
  if(ok){document.getElementById('ki').style.borderColor='var(--correct)';gs.score+=15;S.streak++;S.maxStreak=Math.max(S.maxStreak,S.streak);S.wordsLearned++;
    const set=gs.ktype==='hira'?S.hiraLearned:S.kataLearned;set.add(q.ro);
    addXP(15);spawnPt('⚡',3);showFb(true,`${q.jp} = ${q.ro} ✅`);}
  else{document.getElementById('ki').style.borderColor='var(--wrong)';gs.lives--;S.streak=0;addMistake({jp:q.jp,ro:q.ro,fr:q.ro});showFb(false,`${q.jp} se prononce "${q.ro}"`,val?`Tu as écrit : "${val}"`:'' );}
  updateUI();document.getElementById('nb').classList.add('show');
}
function nextKana(){
  const gs=S.gs;clearInterval(gs.timerInt);gs.idx++;gs.answered=false;
  if(gs.idx>=gs.qs.length||gs.lives<=0)endGame(gs.score,gs.qs.length,'kata_game',gs.ktype);
  else renderKataGame();
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// MEMORY
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function startMemo(){
  const pool=Object.values(COURSES).flatMap(c=>c.words).sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5).slice(0,6);
  const cards=[...pool.map(p=>({...p,side:'jp'})),...pool.map(p=>({...p,side:'fr'}))].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5);
  S.gs={type:'memo',cards,flipped:[],matched:0,moves:0,done:false};renderMemo();
}
function renderMemo(){
  const gs=S.gs;
  document.getElementById('gameWrap').innerHTML=`
    <div class="gh">
      <button class="g-back" onclick="showView('home')">← Quitter</button>
      <div class="g-ta"><div class="g-ti">🃏 Mémory</div><div class="g-su">Associe les paires</div></div>
      <div style="font-size:0.7rem;color:var(--muted)">Coups : <strong id="mvs">0</strong></div>
    </div>
    <div class="mg" id="mg">
      ${gs.cards.map((c,i)=>`<div class="mc" id="mc${i}" onclick="flipMemo(${i})">
        <span class="mch">${c.side==='jp'?c.jp:c.fr}</span>
      </div>`).join('')}
    </div>
    <div class="fb" id="fb"></div>`;
}
function flipMemo(idx){
  const gs=S.gs;if(gs.done)return;
  const el=document.getElementById(`mc${idx}`);
  if(!el||el.classList.contains('match')||el.classList.contains('flip'))return;
  if(gs.flipped.length>=2)return;
  el.classList.add('flip');
  el.innerHTML=`<span>${gs.cards[idx].side==='jp'?gs.cards[idx].jp:gs.cards[idx].fr}</span>`;
  gs.flipped.push(idx);
  if(gs.flipped.length===2){
    gs.moves++;document.getElementById('mvs').textContent=gs.moves;
    const[a,b]=gs.flipped;const ca=gs.cards[a],cb=gs.cards[b];
    const match=ca.ro===cb.ro&&ca.side!==cb.side;
    setTimeout(()=>{
      if(match){
        document.getElementById(`mc${a}`).classList.add('match');
        document.getElementById(`mc${b}`).classList.add('match');
        gs.matched++;spawnPt('🌸',2);
        if(gs.matched===gs.cards.length/2){gs.done=true;const xp=Math.max(20,80-gs.moves*3);addXP(xp);setTimeout(()=>endGame(xp,6,'memo','all'),700);}
      } else {
        [a,b].forEach(i=>{const el=document.getElementById(`mc${i}`);el.classList.add('bad');
          setTimeout(()=>{el.classList.remove('flip','bad');el.innerHTML=`<span class="mch">${gs.cards[i].side==='jp'?gs.cards[i].jp:gs.cards[i].fr}</span>`;},650);});
      }
      gs.flipped=[];
    },520);
  }
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ORDER
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function startOrder(theme){
  const pool=theme==='all'?Object.values(COURSES).flatMap(c=>c.words):(COURSES[theme]?.words||[]);
  const qs=pool.filter(w=>w.jp.length>=3&&w.jp.length<=6).sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5).slice(0,5);
  S.gs={type:'order',qs,idx:0,score:0,lives:3,selected:[],answered:false,theme};renderOrder();
}
function renderOrder(){
  const gs=S.gs;const q=gs.qs[gs.idx];
  const letters=q.jp.split('').sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5);
  gs.letters=letters;gs.selected=[];
  document.getElementById('gameWrap').innerHTML=`
    ${gHeader('🔀 Mot Mélangé',gs.idx+1,gs.qs.length,gs.lives)}
    <div class="gpb"><div class="gpf" style="width:${(gs.idx/gs.qs.length)*100}%"></div></div>
    <div class="qc"><div class="qt red">● RECONSTITUE</div>
      <div class="q-ctr"><div class="q-ctx">Signification : <strong>${q.fr}</strong></div><div class="q-ro">(${q.ro})</div></div>
      <div class="ord-ans" id="oa" onclick="clearOrder()"> </div>
      <div class="lr" id="lr">${letters.map((l,i)=>`<button class="lb" id="lb${i}" onclick="pickLetter(${i},'${l}')">${l}</button>`).join('')}</div>
    </div>
    <div class="fb" id="fb"></div>
    <button class="nb" id="nb" onclick="nextOrder()">SUIVANT →</button>`;
}
function pickLetter(idx,l){
  const gs=S.gs;if(gs.answered)return;
  const btn=document.getElementById(`lb${idx}`);if(btn.disabled)return;
  btn.disabled=true;btn.style.opacity='0.18';
  gs.selected.push({idx,l});
  document.getElementById('oa').textContent=gs.selected.map(s=>s.l).join('');
  const q=gs.qs[gs.idx];
  if(gs.selected.length===q.jp.length){
    gs.answered=true;const attempt=gs.selected.map(s=>s.l).join('');
    if(attempt===q.jp){
      document.getElementById('oa').style.borderColor='var(--correct)';document.getElementById('oa').style.color='var(--correct)';
      gs.score+=12;S.wordsLearned++;addXP(12);spawnPt('🌸',3);showFb(true,`${q.jp} (${q.ro}) = ${q.fr} ✅`);
    } else {
      document.getElementById('oa').style.borderColor='var(--wrong)';document.getElementById('oa').style.color='var(--wrong)';
      gs.lives--;S.streak=0;addMistake(q);showFb(false,`La réponse était : ${q.jp} (${q.ro})`);
    }
    updateUI();document.getElementById('nb').classList.add('show');
  }
}
function clearOrder(){
  const gs=S.gs;if(gs.answered)return;
  gs.selected=[];gs.letters.forEach((_,i)=>{const b=document.getElementById(`lb${i}`);if(b){b.disabled=false;b.style.opacity='1';}});
  document.getElementById('oa').innerHTML=' ';
}
function nextOrder(){
  const gs=S.gs;gs.idx++;gs.answered=false;
  if(gs.idx>=gs.qs.length||gs.lives<=0)endGame(gs.score,gs.qs.length,'order',gs.theme);
  else renderOrder();
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// FLASH
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function startFlash(){S.gs={type:'flash',qs:[...FLASH_QS].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5),idx:0,score:0,lives:3,answered:false};renderFlash();}
function renderFlash(){
  const gs=S.gs;const q=gs.qs[gs.idx];
  const opts=[q.m,...q.w].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5);
  document.getElementById('gameWrap').innerHTML=`
    ${gHeader('👁️ Flash Kanji',gs.idx+1,gs.qs.length,gs.lives)}
    <div class="gpb"><div class="gpf" style="width:${(gs.idx/gs.qs.length)*100}%"></div></div>
    <div class="qc" style="text-align:center"><div class="qt red">● MÉMORISE</div>
      <div id="fk" style="font-family:'Noto Sans JP',sans-serif;font-size:4.5rem;font-weight:900;color:var(--red);padding:16px;transition:opacity 0.5s">${q.k}</div>
      <div id="fks" style="font-size:0.62rem;color:var(--muted);letter-spacing:2px">Retiens ce kanji…</div>
    </div>`;
  setTimeout(()=>{
    const el=document.getElementById('fk');if(!el)return;
    el.style.opacity='0';document.getElementById('fks').textContent='Que signifiait-il ?';
    setTimeout(()=>{
      document.getElementById('gameWrap').innerHTML+=`
        <div class="og" style="margin-top:12px">
          ${opts.map(o=>`<button class="opt" onclick="ansFlash('${o}','${q.m}',this)"><span class="oj" style="font-size:0.9rem">${o}</span></button>`).join('')}
        </div>
        <div class="fb" id="fb"></div>
        <button class="nb" id="nb" onclick="nextFlash()">SUIVANT →</button>`;
    },350);
  },1500);
}
function ansFlash(chosen,correct,btn){
  const gs=S.gs;if(gs.answered)return;gs.answered=true;
  const q=gs.qs[gs.idx];
  document.querySelectorAll('.opt').forEach(b=>b.disabled=true);
  if(chosen===correct){btn.classList.add('ok');gs.score+=q.xp;S.wordsLearned++;addXP(q.xp);spawnPt('⚡',3);showFb(true,`${q.k} = ${q.m} ✅`);}
  else{btn.classList.add('bad');document.querySelectorAll('.opt').forEach(b=>{if(b.querySelector('.oj')?.textContent===correct)b.classList.add('ok');});
    gs.lives--;S.streak=0;addMistake({jp:q.k,ro:q.m.toLowerCase(),fr:q.m});showFb(false,`${q.k} signifie "${q.m}"`);}
  updateUI();document.getElementById('nb').classList.add('show');
}
function nextFlash(){
  const gs=S.gs;gs.idx++;gs.answered=false;
  if(gs.idx>=gs.qs.length||gs.lives<=0)endGame(gs.score,gs.qs.length,'flash','all');
  else renderFlash();
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// KANJI QUIZ
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function startKanjiQuiz(){
  const qs=[...KANJI_LIST].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5).slice(0,10).map(kj=>{
    const wrongs=KANJI_LIST.filter(x=>x.fr!==kj.fr).sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5).slice(0,3);
    const opts=[...wrongs,kj].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5);
    return{kj,opts,correct:opts.findIndex(o=>o.fr===kj.fr),xp:18};
  });
  S.gs={type:'kq',qs,idx:0,score:0,lives:3,answered:false};renderKanjiQuiz();
}
function renderKanjiQuiz(){
  const gs=S.gs;const q=gs.qs[gs.idx];
  document.getElementById('gameWrap').innerHTML=`
    ${gHeader('漢 Quiz Kanji',gs.idx+1,gs.qs.length,gs.lives)}
    <div class="gpb"><div class="gpf" style="width:${(gs.idx/gs.qs.length)*100}%"></div></div>
    <div class="qc" style="border-color:rgba(123,79,158,0.2)"><div class="qt violet">● KANJI · +18 XP</div>
      <div class="q-ctr">
        <div class="q-ctx">Que signifie ce kanji ?</div>
        <div class="q-w" style="font-size:4.5rem;color:var(--violet)">${q.kj.k}</div>
        <div class="q-ro">${q.kj.on} · ${q.kj.kun}</div>
        ${audioBtn(q.kj.k)}
      </div>
      <div class="og">${q.opts.map((o,i)=>`<button class="opt" id="o${i}" onclick="ansKanjiQ(${i})">
        <span class="oj" style="font-size:0.88rem">${o.fr}</span>
      </button>`).join('')}</div>
    </div>
    <div class="fb" id="fb"></div>
    <button class="nb" id="nb" onclick="nextKanjiQ()">SUIVANT →</button>`;
  setTimeout(()=>speakJP(q.kj.k),300);
}
function ansKanjiQ(i){
  const gs=S.gs;if(gs.answered)return;
  doubleTap(i,()=>{
    gs.answered=true;
    const q=gs.qs[gs.idx];
    document.querySelectorAll('.opt').forEach(b=>b.disabled=true);
    if(i===q.correct){
      document.getElementById(`o${i}`).classList.add('ok');
      gs.score+=q.xp;S.streak++;S.maxStreak=Math.max(S.maxStreak,S.streak);S.wordsLearned++;
      S.kanjiLearned.add(q.kj.k);addXP(q.xp);spawnPt('漢',3);
      showFb(true,`${q.kj.k} = ${q.kj.fr} — ${q.kj.ex.split('·')[0].trim()}`);
    } else {
      document.getElementById(`o${i}`).classList.add('bad');document.getElementById(`o${q.correct}`).classList.add('ok');
      gs.lives--;S.streak=0;addMistake({jp:q.kj.k,ro:q.kj.kun.split('・')[0],fr:q.kj.fr});
      showFb(false,`${q.kj.k} signifie "${q.kj.fr}"`,`Lecture : ${q.kj.on} / ${q.kj.kun}`);
    }
    updateUI();buildKanjiView();document.getElementById('nb').classList.add('show');
    setTimeout(()=>{if(document.getElementById('nb'))nextKanjiQ();},1400);
  });
}
function nextKanjiQ(){
  const gs=S.gs;gs.idx++;gs.answered=false;
  if(gs.idx>=gs.qs.length||gs.lives<=0)endGame(gs.score,gs.qs.length,'kanji_quiz','all');
  else renderKanjiQuiz();
}

function startAudioGame(theme){
  const pool=theme==='all'?Object.values(COURSES).flatMap(c=>c.words):(COURSES[theme]?.words||[]);
  const qs=[...pool].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5).slice(0,10).map(w=>{
    const wrongs=pool.filter(x=>x.fr!==w.fr).sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5).slice(0,3);
    const opts=[...wrongs,w].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5);
    return{word:w,opts,correct:opts.findIndex(o=>o.fr===w.fr),xp:15};
  });
  S.gs={type:'audio',qs,idx:0,score:0,lives:3,answered:false,theme};renderAudioGame();
}
function renderAudioGame(){
  const gs=S.gs;const q=gs.qs[gs.idx];
  document.getElementById('gameWrap').innerHTML=`
    ${gHeader('🔊 Mode Audio',gs.idx+1,gs.qs.length,gs.lives)}
    <div class="gpb"><div class="gpf" style="width:${(gs.idx/gs.qs.length)*100}%"></div></div>
    <div class="qc" style="border-color:rgba(45,95,166,0.2)"><div class="qt blue">● ÉCOUTE</div>
      <div class="q-ctr">
        <div class="q-ctx">Quel mot as-tu entendu ?</div>
        <div class="audio-game-display" style="max-width:200px;margin:0 auto 10px">
          <button class="audio-play-btn" id="playBtn" onclick="playAudioWord()">🔊</button>
          <div class="audio-hint">Appuie pour écouter</div>
          <button class="audio-replay" onclick="playAudioWord()">↩ Réécouter</button>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="og" style="margin-top:14px">${q.opts.map((o,i)=>`<button class="opt" id="o${i}" onclick="ansAudio(${i})">
        <span class="oj" style="font-size:0.88rem">${o.fr}</span><span class="of">${o.jp}</span>
      </button>`).join('')}</div>
    </div>
    <div class="fb" id="fb"></div>
    <button class="nb" id="nb" onclick="nextAudio()">SUIVANT →</button>`;
  setTimeout(()=>playAudioWord(),500);
}
function playAudioWord(){
  const gs=S.gs;const q=gs.qs[gs.idx];
  const btn=document.getElementById('playBtn');
  if(btn){btn.classList.add('playing');setTimeout(()=>btn.classList.remove('playing'),1600);}
  speakJP(q.word.jp);
}
function ansAudio(i){
  const gs=S.gs;if(gs.answered)return;
  doubleTap(i,()=>{
    gs.answered=true;const q=gs.qs[gs.idx];
    document.querySelectorAll('.opt').forEach(b=>b.disabled=true);
    if(i===q.correct){
      document.getElementById(`o${i}`).classList.add('ok');
      gs.score+=q.xp;S.streak++;S.maxStreak=Math.max(S.maxStreak,S.streak);S.wordsLearned++;
      srsAddWord(q.word);srsAnswer(q.word.ro,true);
      addXP(q.xp);spawnPt('🔊',3);showFb(true,`${q.word.jp} (${q.word.ro}) = ${q.word.fr} ✅`);speakJP(q.word.jp);
    } else {
      document.getElementById(`o${i}`).classList.add('bad');document.getElementById(`o${q.correct}`).classList.add('ok');
      gs.lives--;S.streak=0;addMistake(q.word);srsAnswer(q.word.ro,false);
      showFb(false,`C'était : ${q.word.jp} (${q.word.ro}) = ${q.word.fr}`);speakJP(q.word.jp);
    }
    updateUI();document.getElementById('nb').classList.add('show');
    setTimeout(()=>{if(document.getElementById('nb'))nextAudio();},1600);
  });
}
function nextAudio(){
  const gs=S.gs;gs.idx++;gs.answered=false;
  if(gs.idx>=gs.qs.length||gs.lives<=0)endGame(gs.score,gs.qs.length,'audio_game',gs.theme);
  else renderAudioGame();
}

function startSRSReview(){
  const due=srsGetDue();
  if(due.length===0){
    document.getElementById('gameWrap').innerHTML=`
      <div class="es">
        <div class="es-ring">🌸</div>
        <div class="es-title">Tout est à jour !</div>
        <div class="es-msg">Aucun mot à réviser pour l'instant.<br>Reviens plus tard !</div>
        <div class="es-btns"><button class="btn-s" onclick="showView('home')">Accueil</button></div>
      </div>`;return;
  }
  const pool=Object.values(COURSES).flatMap(c=>c.words);
  const qs=due.sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5).slice(0,10).map(w=>{
    const wrongs=pool.filter(x=>x.fr!==w.fr).sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5).slice(0,3);
    const opts=[...wrongs,w].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5);
    return{word:w,opts,correct:opts.findIndex(o=>o.fr===w.fr),xp:20};
  });
  S.gs={type:'srs',qs,idx:0,score:0,lives:4,answered:false};renderSRSReview();
}
function renderSRSReview(){
  const gs=S.gs;const q=gs.qs[gs.idx];
  const w=q.word;const lvName=SRS_NAMES[w.level||0];
  document.getElementById('gameWrap').innerHTML=`
    ${gHeader('🗓️ Révision SRS',gs.idx+1,gs.qs.length,gs.lives)}
    <div class="gpb"><div class="gpf" style="width:${(gs.idx/gs.qs.length)*100}%"></div></div>
    <div class="qc" style="border-color:rgba(200,134,10,0.22)">
      <div class="qt gold">● SRS · ${lvName} → ? · +20 XP</div>
      <div class="q-ctr">
        <div class="q-ctx">Niveau actuel : <strong style="color:var(--gold)">${lvName}</strong></div>
        <div class="q-w">${w.jp}</div>
        <div class="q-ro">${w.ro}</div>
        ${audioBtn(w.jp)}
      </div>
      <div class="og">${q.opts.map((o,i)=>`<button class="opt" id="o${i}" onclick="ansSRS(${i})">
        <span class="oj">${o.jp}</span><span class="of">${o.fr}</span>
      </button>`).join('')}</div>
    </div>
    <div class="fb" id="fb"></div>
    <button class="nb" id="nb" onclick="nextSRS()">SUIVANT →</button>`;
}
function ansSRS(i){
  const gs=S.gs;if(gs.answered)return;
  doubleTap(i,()=>{
    gs.answered=true;const q=gs.qs[gs.idx];const w=q.word;
    document.querySelectorAll('.opt').forEach(b=>b.disabled=true);
    if(i===q.correct){
      document.getElementById(`o${i}`).classList.add('ok');
      gs.score+=q.xp;S.streak++;S.maxStreak=Math.max(S.maxStreak,S.streak);S.wordsLearned++;
      srsAnswer(w.ro,true);
      const newLv=SRS_NAMES[S.srs[w.ro]?.level||0];
      addXP(q.xp);spawnPt('⭐',3);showFb(true,`${w.jp} = ${w.fr} ✅ — Niveau : ${newLv}`);
    } else {
      document.getElementById(`o${i}`).classList.add('bad');document.getElementById(`o${q.correct}`).classList.add('ok');
      gs.lives--;S.streak=0;srsAnswer(w.ro,false);
      showFb(false,`${w.jp} (${w.ro}) = ${w.fr}`,`Niveau redescendu…`);
    }
    updateUI();document.getElementById('nb').classList.add('show');
    setTimeout(()=>{if(document.getElementById('nb')){updateSRSBadge();nextSRS();}},1400);
  });
}
function nextSRS(){
  const gs=S.gs;gs.idx++;gs.answered=false;
  if(gs.idx>=gs.qs.length||gs.lives<=0){updateSRSBadge();endGame(gs.score,gs.qs.length,'srs_review','all');}
  else renderSRSReview();
}

function startMistakesQuiz(){
  const pool=Object.values(S.mistakes);
  if(pool.length===0){
    document.getElementById('gameWrap').innerHTML=`
      <div class="es"><div class="es-ring">🌸</div><div class="es-title">Aucune erreur !</div>

        <div class="es-btns"><button class="btn-s" onclick="showView('home')">Accueil</button></div></div>`;return;
  }
  const allWords=Object.values(COURSES).flatMap(c=>c.words);
  const qs=pool.sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5).slice(0,10).map(w=>{
    const wrongs=allWords.filter(x=>x.fr!==w.fr).sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5).slice(0,3);
    const opts=[...wrongs,w].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5);
    return{word:w,opts,correct:opts.findIndex(o=>o.fr===w.fr),xp:18};
  });
  S.gs={type:'mq',qs,idx:0,score:0,lives:3,answered:false};renderMQ();
}
function renderMQ(){
  const gs=S.gs;const q=gs.qs[gs.idx];
  document.getElementById('gameWrap').innerHTML=`
    ${gHeader('❌ Révision Erreurs',gs.idx+1,gs.qs.length,gs.lives)}

    <div class="qc" style="border-color:rgba(192,57,43,0.2)"><div class="qt red">● ERREURS · +18 XP</div>
      <div class="q-ctr">
        <div class="q-ctx">Tu t'étais trompé — souviens-toi !</div>
        <div class="q-w">${q.word.jp}</div>
        <div class="q-ro">${q.word.ro}</div>
        ${audioBtn(q.word.jp)}
      </div>
      <div class="og">${q.opts.map((o,i)=>`<button class="opt" id="o${i}" onclick="ansMQ(${i})">
        <span class="oj">${o.jp}</span><span class="of">${o.fr}</span>
      </button>`).join('')}</div>
    </div>
    <div class="fb" id="fb"></div>
    <button class="nb" id="nb" onclick="nextMQ()">SUIVANT →</button>`;
}
function ansMQ(i){
  const gs=S.gs;if(gs.answered)return;
  doubleTap(i,()=>{
    gs.answered=true;const q=gs.qs[gs.idx];
    document.querySelectorAll('.opt').forEach(b=>b.disabled=true);
    if(i===q.correct){
      document.getElementById(`o${i}`).classList.add('ok');
      gs.score+=q.xp;S.streak++;S.maxStreak=Math.max(S.maxStreak,S.streak);
      removeMistake(q.word.ro);srsAnswer(q.word.ro,true);
      addXP(q.xp);spawnPt('🌟',4);showFb(true,`Bravo ! Erreur corrigée ✅`);
    } else {
      document.getElementById(`o${i}`).classList.add('bad');document.getElementById(`o${q.correct}`).classList.add('ok');
      gs.lives--;S.streak=0;S.mistakes[q.word.ro].count++;srsAnswer(q.word.ro,false);
      showFb(false,`${q.word.jp} (${q.word.ro}) = ${q.word.fr}`);
    }
    updateUI();document.getElementById('nb').classList.add('show');
    setTimeout(()=>{if(document.getElementById('nb'))nextMQ();},1400);
  });
}
function nextMQ(){
  const gs=S.gs;gs.idx++;gs.answered=false;
  if(gs.idx>=gs.qs.length||gs.lives<=0)endGame(gs.score,gs.qs.length,'mistakes_quiz','all');
  else renderMQ();
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SHARED HELPERS
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function gHeader(title,cur,total,lives){
  return`<div class="gh">
    <button class="g-back" onclick="showView('home')">← Quitter</button>
    <div class="g-ta"><div class="g-ti">${title}</div><div class="g-su">${cur} / ${total}</div></div>
    <div class="lives">${[0,1,2].map(i=>`<span class="lf ${i>=lives?'gone':''}">❤️</span>`).join('')}</div>
  </div>`;
}
function showFb(ok,msg,extra=''){
  const el=document.getElementById('fb');if(!el)return;
  el.className=`fb show ${ok?'ok':'bad'}`;
  el.innerHTML=`<div class="fb-t">${ok?'正解！ ✓':'惜しい… ✗'}</div>${msg}${extra?`<div class="fb-x">${extra}</div>`:''}`;
}
function endGame(score,total,type,theme){
  const mk=Object.keys(S.mistakes).length;
  const grade=score>=160?'完璧！':score>=110?'素晴らしい！':score>=60?'よかった！':'続けよう！';
  const flavor=score>=160?'Performance parfaite, tu es incroyable 🌸':
    score>=110?'Excellent travail ! Tu maîtrises bien ce vocabulaire.':
    score>=60?'Bonne session ! Rejoue pour progresser.':'Chaque erreur est une leçon. Courage !';
  document.getElementById('gameWrap').innerHTML=`
    <div class="es">
      <div class="es-ring">${S.char.icon}</div>
      <div class="es-title">${grade}</div>
      <span class="es-xp">+${score} XP</span>
      <div class="es-msg">${flavor}</div>
      <div class="es-tot">XP total : <span>${S.xp}</span> · Niveau <span>${S.level}</span></div>
      ${mk>0?`<div style="background:rgba(192,57,43,0.06);border:1.5px solid rgba(192,57,43,0.15);border-radius:10px;padding:10px;font-size:0.7rem;color:var(--wrong);margin-bottom:14px">
        ❌ ${mk} mot${mk>1?'s':''} dans ta banque d'erreurs
      </div>`:''}
      <div class="es-btns">
        <button class="btn-r" onclick="launchGame('${type}','${theme}')">▶ Rejouer</button>
        ${mk>0?`<button class="btn-mb" onclick="launchGame('mistakes_quiz','all')">❌ Réviser</button>`:''}
        <button class="btn-s" onclick="showView('home')">Accueil</button>
      </div>
    </div>`;
}
function spawnPt(emoji,n=3){
  for(let i=0;i<n;i++)setTimeout(()=>{
    const p=document.createElement('div');p.className='pt';p.textContent=emoji;
    p.style.left=(20+Math.random()*60)+'vw';p.style.top=(30+Math.random()*30)+'vh';
    document.body.appendChild(p);setTimeout(()=>p.remove(),1100);
  },i*150);
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SAUVEGARDE — Code texte à copier/coller
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function serializeState(){
  const d={
    v:9,
    char:S.char, goal:S.goal,
    xp:S.xp, level:S.level, streak:S.streak, maxStreak:S.maxStreak,
    wordsLearned:S.wordsLearned, gamesPlayed:S.gamesPlayed,
    prog:Object.fromEntries(Object.entries(S.progress).map(([k,v])=>[k,[...v]])),
    hira:[...S.hiraLearned], kata:[...S.kataLearned],
    kanji:[...S.kanjiLearned],
    phrases:[...(S.phrasesLearned||new Set())],
    mistakes:S.mistakes,
    srs:Object.fromEntries(Object.entries(S.srs).map(([k,v])=>[k,{...v,nextReview:v.nextReview}])),
    story:S.storyProgress,
    trophies:S.trophies||{},
    quests:S.quests||null,
  };
  return btoa(unescape(encodeURIComponent(JSON.stringify(d))));
}

function deserializeState(code){
  try{
    const d=JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(escape(atob(code.trim()))));
    if(!d||(d.v!==9&&d.v!==8)) return false;
    S.char=d.char; S.goal=d.goal;
    S.xp=d.xp; S.level=d.level; S.streak=d.streak||0; S.maxStreak=d.maxStreak||0;
    S.wordsLearned=d.wordsLearned||0; S.gamesPlayed=d.gamesPlayed||0;
    S.progress={};
    Object.keys(COURSES).forEach(k=>S.progress[k]=new Set(d.prog?.[k]||[]));
    S.hiraLearned=new Set(d.hira||[]);
    S.kataLearned=new Set(d.kata||[]);
    S.kanjiLearned=new Set(d.kanji||[]);
    S.phrasesLearned=new Set(d.phrases||[]);
    S.mistakes=d.mistakes||{};
    S.srs={};
    Object.entries(d.srs||{}).forEach(([k,v])=>{ S.srs[k]={...v}; });
    S.storyProgress=d.story||{};
    S.trophies=d.trophies||{};
    S.quests=d.quests||null;
    return true;
  } catch(e){ return false; }
}

function showSaveModal(){
  const code=serializeState();
  const ov=document.createElement('div');
  ov.id='saveOverlay';
  ov.style.cssText='position:fixed;inset:0;background:rgba(100,50,0,0.45);z-index:9000;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;padding:20px;backdrop-filter:blur(4px)';
  ov.innerHTML=`
    <div style="background:var(--surface);border:2px solid var(--border2);border-radius:22px;padding:28px;max-width:480px;width:100%;position:relative;box-shadow:0 24px 80px rgba(100,50,0,0.2)">
      <button onclick="document.getElementById('saveOverlay').remove()" style="position:absolute;top:12px;right:14px;background:none;border:none;color:var(--muted2);font-size:1.2rem;cursor:pointer">✕</button>
      <div style="font-family:'Kaisei Decol',serif;font-size:1.1rem;color:var(--red);margin-bottom:4px">💾 Sauvegarder la progression</div>
      <div style="font-size:0.66rem;color:var(--muted);margin-bottom:16px">Copie ce code et garde-le précieusement. Colle-le pour reprendre plus tard.</div>

      <div style="margin-bottom:18px">
        <div style="font-size:0.62rem;color:var(--muted);letter-spacing:2px;margin-bottom:6px">TON CODE DE SAUVEGARDE</div>
        <textarea id="saveCode" readonly style="width:100%;height:90px;background:var(--cream);border:1.5px solid var(--border2);border-radius:10px;padding:10px;font-family:'DM Mono',monospace;font-size:0.62rem;color:var(--text);resize:none;line-height:1.5">${code}</textarea>

      document.getElementById('saveCode').select();
      document.execCommand('copy');
      this.textContent='✅ Copié !';

  <div style="margin-top:16px;background:rgba(42,122,111,0.06);border:1px solid rgba(42,122,111,0.18);border-radius:10px;padding:12px;font-size:0.64rem;color:var(--teal);line-height:1.8">

  </div>
</div>`;

document.body.appendChild(ov);
// select the code on click
document.getElementById(‘saveCode’).addEventListener(‘focus’,function(){this.select();});

function loadSave(){
const code=document.getElementById(‘loadCode’).value.trim();
const msg=document.getElementById(‘loadMsg’);
if(!code){msg.style.color=‘var(–wrong)’;msg.textContent=‘⚠️ Colle un code d'abord !’;return;}
if(deserializeState(code)){
msg.style.color=‘var(–correct)’;
msg.textContent=‘✅ Sauvegarde chargée ! Actualisation…’;
setTimeout(()=>{
document.getElementById(‘saveOverlay’).remove();
buildSidebar();buildHomeGames();buildCoursesHome();
buildHiraView();buildKataRefView();buildKanjiView();
buildStoryMap();updateUI();showView(‘home’);
},1000);
} else {
msg.style.color=‘var(–wrong)’;
msg.textContent=‘❌ Code invalide — vérifie que tu as tout copié.’;
}
}

{q:‘Pour faire du 🍵 matcha latte, il faut ?’,correct:‘matcha + miruku’,opts:[‘matcha + miruku’,‘kohi + sato’,‘mugicha + mizu’,‘sake + yu’],expl:‘抹茶ラテ = matcha en poudre + lait (ミルク) !’},

{q:‘Le 🍙 onigiri c'est fait avec ?’,correct:‘kome + nori’,opts:[‘kome + nori’,‘pan + bata’,‘udon + dashi’,‘tofu + miso’],expl:‘おにぎり = riz (米) enroulé dans algue (海苔) !’},
{q:‘Pour faire de la soupe 🥣 miso, on a besoin de ?’,correct:‘miso + tofu + dashi’,opts:[‘miso + tofu + dashi’,‘shoyu + niku + negi’,‘sake + yasai + men’,‘kome + nori + sakana’],expl:‘味噌汁 = miso + tofu + bouillon dashi !’},

{q:‘Pour faire des 🍡 dango, on utilise ?’,correct:‘komeko’,opts:[‘komeko’,‘komugi’,‘sato’,‘katakuriko’],expl:‘団子 = farine de riz (米粉 = komeko) !’},
{q:‘Le 🫕 nabe (fondue japonaise) contient ?’,correct:‘yasai + niku + tofu’,opts:[‘yasai + niku + tofu’,‘gohan + tamago + nori’,‘men + kare + bata’,‘sakana + miso + pan’],expl:‘鍋 = légumes (野菜) + viande (肉) + tofu dans bouillon !’},
