let cuisineSt={qs:[],idx:0,score:0,lives:3,answered:false};
function startCuisine(){
cuisineSt={qs:[…CUISINE_QS].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5),idx:0,score:0,lives:3,answered:false};
renderCuisine();
}
function renderCuisine(){
const gs=cuisineSt;const q=gs.qs[gs.idx];
if(!q){endCuisine();return;}
document.getElementById(‘gameWrap’).innerHTML=` ${gHeader('🍣 Cuisine Japonaise',gs.idx+1,gs.qs.length,gs.lives)} <div class="gpb"><div class="gpf" style="width:${(gs.idx/gs.qs.length)*100}%"></div></div> <div class="qc"> <div class="qt teal">🍱 CUISINE JAPONAISE</div> <div class="q-ctr" style="margin-bottom:16px"> <div style="font-weight:800;font-size:1rem;color:var(--text);line-height:1.4;text-align:center">${q.q}</div> </div> <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:8px"> ${q.opts.map((o,i)=>`<button class="opt" id="cq${i}" onclick="ansCuisine(${i})">
<span style="font-family:'DM Mono',monospace;font-size:0.78rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--red)">${o}</span>
</button>`).join('')} </div> </div> <div class="fb" id="fb"></div> <button class="nb" id="nb" onclick="nextCuisine()">SUIVANT →</button>`;
}
function ansCuisine(i){
if(cuisineSt.answered)return;cuisineSt.answered=true;
const q=cuisineSt.qs[cuisineSt.idx];
document.querySelectorAll(’[id^=cq]’).forEach(b=>b.disabled=true);
const ok=q.opts[i]===q.correct;
document.getElementById(`cq${i}`).classList.add(ok?‘ok’:‘bad’);
if(!ok) q.opts.forEach((o,j)=>{if(o===q.correct)document.getElementById(`cq${j}`).classList.add(‘ok’);});
if(ok){cuisineSt.score++;S.streak++;S.maxStreak=Math.max(S.maxStreak,S.streak);addXP(15);spawnPt(‘🍣’,3);showFb(true,q.expl);}
else{cuisineSt.lives–;S.streak=0;showFb(false,q.expl);}
document.getElementById(‘nb’).classList.add(‘show’);updateUI();
setTimeout(nextCuisine,1600);
}
function nextCuisine(){cuisineSt.idx++;cuisineSt.answered=false;if(cuisineSt.idx>=cuisineSt.qs.length||cuisineSt.lives<=0)endCuisine();else renderCuisine();}
function endCuisine(){
document.getElementById(‘gameWrap’).innerHTML=`<div class="es"> <div class="es-ring">🍣</div><div class="es-title">Itadakimasu !</div> <span class="es-xp">${cuisineSt.score}/${cuisineSt.qs.length}</span> <div class="es-msg">${cuisineSt.score>=8?'🏆 Chef étoilé !':cuisineSt.score>=5?'👨‍🍳 Bon cuisinier !':'🥢 Continue à t\'entraîner !'}</div> <div class="es-btns"><button class="btn-r" onclick="startCuisine()">▶ Rejouer</button> <button class="btn-s" onclick="showView('games')">← Jeux</button></div></div>`;
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// PLUIE DE KANA — mode tap QCM
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
let rainSt={score:0,lives:3,active:false,currentKana:null};
function startRain(){
rainSt={score:0,lives:3,active:true,currentKana:null};
renderRain();
}
function renderRain(){
if(!rainSt.active)return;
const all=[…HIRAGANA,…KATAKANA];
const k=all[Math.floor(Math.random()*all.length)];
rainSt.currentKana=k;
// 3 mauvaises réponses + 1 bonne
const wrongs=all.filter(x=>x.ro!==k.ro).sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5).slice(0,3);
const opts=[…wrongs,k].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5);
const hearts=‘❤️’.repeat(rainSt.lives)+‘🖤’.repeat(3-rainSt.lives);
document.getElementById(‘gameWrap’).innerHTML=` ${gHeader('🌧️ Pluie de Kana',0,0,rainSt.lives)} <div style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:6px"> <span style="font-size:0.62rem;color:var(--muted)">Score : </span> <span style="font-weight:900;color:var(--gold);font-size:1.3rem">${rainSt.score}</span> </div> <div style="text-align:center;background:var(--cream);border:1.5px solid var(--border2);border-radius:16px;padding:28px 16px;margin-bottom:16px;position:relative;overflow:hidden"> <div style="font-size:0.6rem;color:var(--muted);letter-spacing:2px;margin-bottom:8px">QUEL EST CE KANA ?</div> <div style="font-family:'Noto Sans JP',sans-serif;font-size:5rem;font-weight:900;color:var(--red);line-height:1;animation:dropIn 0.3s ease">${k.jp}</div> <div style="font-size:0.58rem;color:var(--muted2);margin-top:8px">${k.jp.charCodeAt(0)>=0x30A0?'Katakana':'Hiragana'}</div> </div> <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:9px"> ${opts.map((o,i)=>`<button class="opt" id="rn${i}" onclick="ansRain('${o.ro}',${i})">
<span style="font-family:'DM Mono',monospace;font-size:1rem;font-weight:800;color:var(--text)">${o.ro}</span>
</button>`).join('')} </div> <div class="fb" id="fb"></div>`;
}
function ansRain(ro,i){
if(!rainSt.active)return;
const k=rainSt.currentKana;
document.querySelectorAll(’[id^=rn]’).forEach(b=>b.disabled=true);
const ok=ro===k.ro;
document.getElementById(`rn${i}`).classList.add(ok?‘ok’:‘bad’);
if(!ok){
// Montre la bonne réponse
document.querySelectorAll(’[id^=rn]’).forEach((b,j)=>{
if(b.querySelector(‘span’).textContent===k.ro)b.classList.add(‘ok’);
});
rainSt.lives–;S.streak=0;
if(rainSt.lives<=0){rainSt.active=false;setTimeout(endRain,1000);return;}
} else {
rainSt.score++;S.streak++;S.maxStreak=Math.max(S.maxStreak,S.streak);
addXP(6);spawnPt(‘🌸’,1);bumpQuest(‘maxStreak’);
}
updateUI();
setTimeout(renderRain,ok?600:1200);
}
function endRain(){
document.getElementById(‘gameWrap’).innerHTML=`<div class="es"> <div class="es-ring">🌧️</div><div class="es-title">Averse terminée !</div> <span class="es-xp">${rainSt.score}</span> <div class="es-msg">${rainSt.score} kana reconnus !${rainSt.score>=20?' 🏆 Incroyable !':rainSt.score>=10?' 👍 Bien joué !':' Continue !'}</div> <div class="es-btns"><button class="btn-r" onclick="startRain()">▶ Rejouer</button> <button class="btn-s" onclick="showView('games')">← Jeux</button></div></div>`;
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// INTRUS
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
let intrusSt={qs:[],idx:0,score:0,lives:3,answered:false};
function buildIntrusQs(){
const courseList=Object.values(COURSES).filter(c=>c.words.length>=4);
return courseList.sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5).slice(0,8).map(c=>{
const trio=[…c.words].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5).slice(0,3);
const other=Object.values(COURSES).filter(x=>x.id!==c.id);
const otherC=other[Math.floor(Math.random()*other.length)];
const intrus=otherC.words[Math.floor(Math.random()*otherC.words.length)];
const opts=[…trio,intrus].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5);
return{cat:c.name,opts,intrusJp:intrus.jp};
});
}
function startIntrus(){
intrusSt={qs:buildIntrusQs(),idx:0,score:0,lives:3,answered:false};
renderIntrus();
}
function renderIntrus(){
const gs=intrusSt;const q=gs.qs[gs.idx];
if(!q){endIntrus();return;}
document.getElementById(‘gameWrap’).innerHTML=` ${gHeader('🔍 L\'Intrus',gs.idx+1,gs.qs.length,gs.lives)} <div class="gpb"><div class="gpf" style="width:${(gs.idx/gs.qs.length)*100}%"></div></div> <div class="qc"> <div class="qt pink">● THÈME : ${q.cat.toUpperCase()}</div> <div class="q-ctr" style="margin-bottom:14px"> <div style="font-weight:800;font-size:0.95rem;color:var(--red)">Quel mot n'appartient PAS à ce thème ?</div> </div> <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:8px"> ${q.opts.map((w,i)=>`<button class="opt" id="io${i}" onclick="ansIntrus(${i})">
<span class="oj">${w.jp}</span><span class="of">${w.fr}</span>
</button>`).join('')} </div> </div> <div class="fb" id="fb"></div> <button class="nb" id="nb" onclick="nextIntrus()">SUIVANT →</button>`;
}
function ansIntrus(i){
if(intrusSt.answered)return;intrusSt.answered=true;
const q=intrusSt.qs[intrusSt.idx];
document.querySelectorAll(’#io0,#io1,#io2,#io3’).forEach(b=>b.disabled=true);
const chosen=q.opts[i];const ok=chosen.jp===q.intrusJp;
document.getElementById(`io${i}`).classList.add(ok?‘ok’:‘bad’);
if(!ok) q.opts.forEach((w,j)=>{if(w.jp===q.intrusJp)document.getElementById(`io${j}`).classList.add(‘ok’);});
if(ok){intrusSt.score++;S.streak++;S.maxStreak=Math.max(S.maxStreak,S.streak);addXP(15);spawnPt(‘🔍’,3);showFb(true,`Exact ! "${chosen.jp}" n'est pas dans le thème "${q.cat}" ✅`);}
else{intrusSt.lives–;S.streak=0;showFb(false,`L'intrus était "${q.intrusJp}" !`);}
document.getElementById(‘nb’).classList.add(‘show’);updateUI();
setTimeout(nextIntrus,1400);
}
function nextIntrus(){intrusSt.idx++;intrusSt.answered=false;if(intrusSt.idx>=intrusSt.qs.length)endIntrus();else renderIntrus();}
function endIntrus(){
document.getElementById(‘gameWrap’).innerHTML=`<div class="es"> <div class="es-ring">🔍</div><div class="es-title">Terminé !</div> <span class="es-xp">${intrusSt.score}/${intrusSt.qs.length}</span> <div class="es-msg">${intrusSt.score} intrus trouvés !</div> <div class="es-btns"><button class="btn-r" onclick="startIntrus()">▶ Rejouer</button> <button class="btn-s" onclick="showView('games')">← Jeux</button></div></div>`;
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// CHRONO 60s
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
let chronoSt={score:0,timeLeft:60,pool:[],idx:0,timer:null,answered:false};
function startChrono(){
clearInterval(chronoSt.timer);
const pool=Object.values(COURSES).flatMap(c=>c.words).sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5);
chronoSt={score:0,timeLeft:60,pool,idx:0,timer:null,answered:false};
renderChrono();
chronoSt.timer=setInterval(()=>{
chronoSt.timeLeft–;
const el=document.getElementById(‘chronoTime’);
if(el){el.textContent=chronoSt.timeLeft;el.style.color=chronoSt.timeLeft<=10?‘var(–wrong)’:‘var(–red)’;}
if(chronoSt.timeLeft<=0){clearInterval(chronoSt.timer);endChrono();}
},1000);
}
function renderChrono(){
const gs=chronoSt;
const w=gs.pool[gs.idx%gs.pool.length];
gs.answered=false;
const wrong=gs.pool.filter(x=>x.fr!==w.fr).sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5).slice(0,3);
const opts=[…wrong,w].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5);
const ci=opts.findIndex(o=>o.fr===w.fr);
document.getElementById(‘gameWrap’).innerHTML=` ${gHeader('⏱️ Chrono 60s',0,0,0)} <div style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:10px"> <div id="chronoTime" style="font-weight:900;font-size:3.2rem;color:var(--red)">${gs.timeLeft}</div> <div style="font-size:0.62rem;color:var(--muted)">Score : <strong style="color:var(--gold);font-size:1rem">${gs.score}</strong></div> </div> <div class="qc" style="margin-bottom:8px"> <div class="q-ctr"><div class="q-w">${w.jp}</div><div class="q-ro">${w.ro}</div></div> <div class="og">${opts.map((o,i)=>`<button class="opt" id="co${i}" onclick="ansChronoOpt(${i},${ci})">
<span class="oj">${o.jp}</span><span class="of">${o.fr}</span>
</button>`).join('')}</div> </div>`;
}
function ansChronoOpt(i,correct){
if(chronoSt.answered||chronoSt.timeLeft<=0)return;
chronoSt.answered=true;
document.querySelectorAll(’.opt’).forEach(b=>b.disabled=true);
document.getElementById(`co${i}`).classList.add(i===correct?‘ok’:‘bad’);
if(i!==correct)document.getElementById(`co${correct}`).classList.add(‘ok’);
if(i===correct){chronoSt.score++;addXP(5);spawnPt(‘⚡’,1);}
chronoSt.idx++;
setTimeout(()=>{if(chronoSt.timeLeft>0)renderChrono();},500);
}
function endChrono(){
clearInterval(chronoSt.timer);
addXP(chronoSt.score*2);
document.getElementById(‘gameWrap’).innerHTML=`<div class="es"> <div class="es-ring">⏱️</div><div class="es-title">Temps écoulé !</div> <span class="es-xp">${chronoSt.score} mots</span> <div class="es-msg">Tu as reconnu ${chronoSt.score} mots en 60 secondes !<br>+${chronoSt.score*2} XP bonus</div> <div class="es-btns"><button class="btn-r" onclick="startChrono()">▶ Rejouer</button> <button class="btn-s" onclick="showView('games')">← Jeux</button></div></div>`;
}

document.head.appendChild(styleNew);

function buildPhrasesView(){
const phH=document.getElementById(‘phrasesHeader’);
const phC=document.getElementById(‘phrasesContent’);
if(!phH||!phC)return;
if(!S.phrasesLearned)S.phrasesLearned=new Set();
const total=PHRASES_CATEGORIES.reduce((a,cat)=>a+cat.phrases.length,0);
const learned=S.phrasesLearned.size;
const pct=Math.round((learned/total)*100);
phH.innerHTML=`<div style="background:linear-gradient(135deg,#e63946,#c0392b);border-radius:20px;padding:20px;margin-bottom:18px;color:white;box-shadow:0 8px 24px rgba(230,57,70,0.25)">
<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:14px">
<div style="font-size:3rem">💬</div>
<div>
<div style="font-size:1.2rem;font-weight:800">100 Phrases de Base</div>
<div style="font-size:0.65rem;opacity:0.85">Tes premieres phrases au Japon</div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="margin-top:12px;height:6px;background:rgba(255,255,255,0.25);border-radius:3px;overflow:hidden">
<div style="width:${pct}%;height:100%;background:white;border-radius:3px;transition:width 0.5s"></div>
</div>
<div style="font-size:0.6rem;opacity:0.8;margin-top:4px">${learned}/${total} phrases apprises - ${pct}%</div>

  </div>`;
  phC.innerHTML=PHRASES_CATEGORIES.map((cat,ci)=>{
    const catL=cat.phrases.filter((_,pi)=>S.phrasesLearned.has(ci+"-"+pi)).length;
    const cards=cat.phrases.map((p,pi)=>{
      const key=ci+"-"+pi;
      const done=S.phrasesLearned.has(key);
      const borderColor=done?'rgba(76,175,130,0.4)':'var(--border)';
      const check=done?'✅':'⬜';
      return `<div onclick="togglePhrase('${key}')" style="background:white;border:2px solid ${borderColor};border-left:4px solid ${cat.color};border-radius:14px;padding:14px;margin-bottom:8px;cursor:pointer;box-shadow:0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.04)">
        <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:flex-start;gap:8px">
          <div style="flex:1">
            <div style="font-size:1.1rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--ink);margin-bottom:2px">${p.jp}</div>
            <div style="font-size:0.7rem;color:var(--teal);font-weight:600;margin-bottom:2px">${p.ro}</div>
            <div style="font-size:0.72rem;color:var(--ink);margin-bottom:4px">${p.fr}</div>
            <div style="font-size:0.6rem;color:var(--muted);background:rgba(0,0,0,0.04);border-radius:6px;padding:3px 7px;display:inline-block">💡 ${p.note}</div>
          </div>
          <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:6px;flex-shrink:0">
            <button onclick="event.stopPropagation();speakJP(this.dataset.t)" data-t="${p.jp}" style="background:rgba(76,175,130,0.12);border:1px solid rgba(76,175,130,0.25);border-radius:8px;padding:5px 8px;font-size:0.75rem;cursor:pointer">🔊</button>
            <div style="text-align:center;font-size:1rem">${check}</div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>`;
    }).join('');
    return `<div style="margin-bottom:18px">
      <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:10px">
        <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px">
          <span style="font-size:1.5rem">${cat.icon}</span>
          <span style="font-size:0.95rem;font-weight:800;color:${cat.color}">${cat.name}</span>
        </div>
        <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px">
          <span style="font-size:0.6rem;color:var(--muted);font-weight:700">${catL}/${cat.phrases.length}</span>
          <button onclick="startPhraseQuiz(${ci})" style="background:${cat.color};color:white;border:none;border-radius:10px;padding:5px 12px;font-size:0.6rem;font-weight:800;cursor:pointer">QUIZ</button>
        </div>
      </div>
      ${cards}
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

function togglePhrase(key){
if(!S.phrasesLearned)S.phrasesLearned=new Set();
if(S.phrasesLearned.has(key)){S.phrasesLearned.delete(key);}
else{S.phrasesLearned.add(key);addXP(5);bumpQuest(‘phrasesLearned’);checkTrophies();}
buildPhrasesView();
}

function startPhraseQuiz(ci){
const cat=PHRASES_CATEGORIES[ci];
const all=PHRASES_CATEGORIES.flatMap(c=>c.phrases);
const qs=[…cat.phrases].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5).slice(0,Math.min(8,cat.phrases.length));
S.gs={type:‘phrasesquiz’,qs,idx:0,score:0,lives:3,answered:false,ci,all};
S.gamesPlayed++;bumpQuest(‘gamesPlayed’);
showView(‘game’);renderPhraseQuiz();
}
function renderPhraseQuiz(){
const gs=S.gs,q=gs.qs[gs.idx];
const wrongs=gs.all.filter(p=>p.fr!==q.fr).sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5).slice(0,3);
const opts=[…wrongs,q].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5);
gs.opts=opts;gs.cor=opts.findIndex(o=>o.fr===q.fr);
document.getElementById(‘gameWrap’).innerHTML=
gHeader(‘💬 Phrases’,gs.idx+1,gs.qs.length,gs.lives)
+’<div class="gpb"><div class="gpf" style="width:'+Math.round(gs.idx/gs.qs.length*100)+'%"></div></div>’
+’<div class="qc" style="border-color:rgba(230,57,70,0.25)">’
+’<div class="qt red">● TRADUCTION</div>’
+’<div class="q-ctr"><div class="q-ctx">Que signifie cette phrase ?</div>’
+’<div class="q-w" style="font-size:1.1rem">’+q.jp+’</div>’
+’<div class="q-ro">’+q.ro+’</div>’
+audioBtn(q.jp)+’</div></div>’
+’<div class="og">’+opts.map((o,i)=>’<button class="opt of" onclick="ansPQ('+i+')">’+o.fr+’</button>’).join(’’)+’</div>’
+’<div class="fb" id="fb"></div>’
+’<button class="nb" id="nb" onclick="nextPQ()">SUIVANT →</button>’;
speakJP(q.jp);
}
function ansPQ(i){
const gs=S.gs;if(gs.answered)return;gs.answered=true;
const q=gs.qs[gs.idx],ok=(i===gs.cor);
document.querySelectorAll(’.opt’).forEach((b,bi)=>{b.classList.add(bi===gs.cor?‘ok’:‘bad’);b.disabled=true;});
if(ok){gs.score+=15;S.streak++;S.maxStreak=Math.max(S.maxStreak,S.streak);addXP(15);spawnPt(‘💬’,4);
if(!S.phrasesLearned)S.phrasesLearned=new Set();
S.phrasesLearned.add(gs.ci+’-’+gs.idx);
showFb(true,q.jp+’ = ’+q.fr,’💡 ‘+q.note);}
else{gs.lives–;S.streak=0;showFb(false,q.jp+’ = ’+q.fr,’💡 ’+q.note);speakJP(q.jp);}
updateUI();document.getElementById(‘nb’).classList.add(‘show’);
}
function nextPQ(){
const gs=S.gs;gs.idx++;gs.answered=false;
if(gs.idx>=gs.qs.length||gs.lives<=0)endGame(gs.score,gs.qs.length,‘phrases’,‘all’);
else renderPhraseQuiz();
}

// ── TRADUCTION ECLAIR ──
function startTraduction(theme){
const pool=Object.values(COURSES).flatMap(c=>c.words);
const qs=[…pool].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5).slice(0,10);
S.gs={type:‘traduction’,qs,idx:0,score:0,lives:3,answered:false,pool};
renderTraduction();
}
function renderTraduction(){
const gs=S.gs,q=gs.qs[gs.idx];
const jpToFr=Math.random()<0.5;
gs.dir=jpToFr;
const question=jpToFr?q.jp:q.fr;
const answer=jpToFr?q.fr:q.jp;
const wrongs=gs.pool.filter(w=>w.fr!==q.fr).sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5).slice(0,3).map(w=>jpToFr?w.fr:w.jp);
const opts=[…wrongs,answer].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5);
gs.opts=opts;gs.cor=opts.indexOf(answer);
document.getElementById(‘gameWrap’).innerHTML=
gHeader(‘🔄 Traduction’,gs.idx+1,gs.qs.length,gs.lives)
+’<div class="gpb"><div class="gpf" style="width:'+Math.round(gs.idx/gs.qs.length*100)+'%"></div></div>’
+’<div class="qc"><div class="qt '+(jpToFr?'teal':'violet')+'">’+(jpToFr?‘🇯🇵 JP → FR’:‘🇫🇷 FR → JP’)+’</div>’
+’<div class="q-ctr"><div class="q-ctx">’+(jpToFr?‘Traduction ?’:‘En japonais ?’)+’</div>’
+’<div class="q-w">’+question+’</div>’
+(jpToFr?’<div class="q-ro">’+q.ro+’</div>’:’’)
+audioBtn(q.jp)+’</div></div>’
+’<div class="og">’+opts.map((o,i)=>’<button class="opt '+(jpToFr?'of':'oj')+'" onclick="ansT('+i+')">’+o+’</button>’).join(’’)+’</div>’
+’<div class="fb" id="fb"></div>’
+’<button class="nb" id="nb" onclick="nextT()">SUIVANT →</button>’;
if(jpToFr)speakJP(q.jp);
}
function ansT(i){
const gs=S.gs;if(gs.answered)return;gs.answered=true;
const q=gs.qs[gs.idx],ok=(i===gs.cor);
document.querySelectorAll(’.opt’).forEach((b,bi)=>{b.classList.add(bi===gs.cor?‘ok’:‘bad’);b.disabled=true;});
if(ok){gs.score+=14;S.streak++;S.maxStreak=Math.max(S.maxStreak,S.streak);S.wordsLearned++;
srsAddWord(q);srsAnswer(q.ro,true);addXP(14);spawnPt(‘🔄’,4);
showFb(true,q.jp+’ (’+q.ro+’) = ‘+q.fr);}
else{gs.lives–;S.streak=0;addMistake(q);srsAnswer(q.ro,false);
showFb(false,q.jp+’ (’+q.ro+’) = ’+q.fr);speakJP(q.jp);}
updateUI();document.getElementById(‘nb’).classList.add(‘show’);
}
function nextT(){
const gs=S.gs;gs.idx++;gs.answered=false;
if(gs.idx>=gs.qs.length||gs.lives<=0)endGame(gs.score,gs.qs.length,‘traduction’,‘all’);
else renderTraduction();
}

</script>
</body>
</html>
